Suzhou Incense Boat Meets Bandits Midway 98

Recently, the wind has been gentle and the sun has been warm. Pilgrims from all over the country have been flocking to Hangzhou to burn incense. On the 6th of this month, there was a case of robbery of an incense boat near Chefang in Su County. Fortunately, the losses were limited. About twenty men and women pilgrims from Changshu County were traveling together on a boat to Hangzhou to burn incense. Yesterday (the 9th) at 7 am, when passing near Pingwang, they suddenly encountered a bandit boat. Seven or eight bandits jumped out, held weapons, and stopped the boat to rob. They searched each pilgrim one by one and robbed them of silver dollars and clothing worth about two hundred gold. The bandits took the stolen goods and fled towards Taihu Lake. The incense boat, due to the robbery of money, returned to Changshu.

Wuxi Power Plant Cook Electrocuted to Death 100

Dang Shengjin, a cook at the Qishuyan Power Plant in the city, was 42 years old and from Tangtou in the northern countryside. He had been serving in the factory for many years. Dang usually lived in an empty house behind the factory's workers' club. The house was equipped with electric lights and wires, which were connected by external leather wires. Recently, because the house was intended to store stoves, Shengjin was about to move out. The wires should have been removed, so at about 11 am yesterday, Shengjin held scissors and cut the wires. Unexpectedly, he was electrocuted on the spot and fell down. He broke his head and fainted on the ground. When a tea servant, Li Jiliang, caught a glimpse, he immediately reported to the general affairs office and summoned a doctor for emergency treatment, but it was ineffective. He died instantly. After the Tu Zheng [local official] reported to the court to come and inspect the scene, he was immediately coffined. It was also said to be a tragic event.

Investigation of Yixing County Magistrate's Accusation Case 101

Gu Tongsun and Gu Liensun, brothers who were heads of field taxation in Yixing County, were arrested for corruption. But on the night of the 16th of last month, they suddenly escaped. Chu Kaiyao, the judicial clerk of the county, also fled in fear of punishment because he had acted as a guarantor for Gu. Zhong Jingcheng, the county magistrate, detained Chu's wife, Shao, in the county for interrogation. Chu's mother, Xu, filed a complaint, and the Suzhou High Court ordered Qian Chengjun, the chief prosecutor of the local branch court in this county, to go to Yixing to verify Shao's injuries and handle the matter according to law. Unexpectedly, County Magistrate Zhong recently detained Gu Tongsun's cousin, Gu Tianmin, in the county, demanding that he hand over Gu Tongsun and Gu Liensun. Because Gu Tianmin firmly refused, he was arrested. He again filed a complaint by telegram. The High Court ordered the local branch court in this county to send Prosecutor Ren Guanghai to Yixing yesterday to review the case files and summon Gu Tianmin for interrogation and handling. He returned to Xixi in the afternoon of the same day.

Nantong Process and Aftermath of Suppressing Maritime Bandits 102

The maritime bandits along the coast of Jiangbei have been completely suppressed. Zheng Yitong, the commander of the Fourth District Security of Nantong, telegraphed the provincial government on the 8th to report on the process of suppressing the maritime bandits and the aftermath, stating that over the past two months, the water public security teams of the three districts had engaged in fierce battles with the bandits, pursued and captured eight bandit ships, destroyed one bandit command ship of the leader Yu Sanduanzi at Sanduanzi, seized 18 guns and 2 cannons, captured five maritime bandits including Zhuang Zhiwei and Fu Xiren alive, and arrested two maritime bandit leaders, Li Shaochun and Xie Weijun. They rescued two female hostages, Wang Zhu's family, three male hostages, over forty boatmen who had been seized, and ten child hostages. They killed over one hundred bandits including the bandit leader Yu Sanduanzi. Our teams successively suffered seven severely wounded senior police officers and one boatman killed in action. Now that the bandits have been wiped out, the following is the progress of the aftermath: (1) Ordering the teams to return to their defenses on a daily basis, and completing the demobilization by March 7; (2) Taozikou and other places are important areas where maritime bandits operate, and it has been decided that the 14th team will send three patrol boats to be stationed and cruise there for a long time, and the Funing security team will station troops at Liuhezhuang for a long time, so as to achieve water and land communication to prevent the resurgence of banditry; (3) Ye Yun had the most bandits who landed and fled, and a special arrest team was formed to hunt them down; (4) In order to maintain permanent security on the water, ships will be borrowed from the coastal fishermen's associations, and troops will be dispatched to patrol the north and south oceans for a long time.

Haimen Wenlin Township Victims Gather to Petition for Relief 103

This county suffered a severe drought last autumn, and the harvest was sharply reduced. At this time of early spring, when the new crop has not yet come in, most of the villagers have run out of food and are crying out for help. The situation is very pitiful. Yesterday (the 7th) morning, over two hundred victims from Wenlin Township in the third district, because they had been out of food for many days and were about to starve to death, went to the home of the township head, Cao Jichang, to request relief. At that time, there were many people speaking at once, causing disturbances. The situation was very tense. The victims gradually dispersed.

Local News

Minister Kong Convened Leaders from All Sectors Yesterday to Discuss Measures to Aid the Market 104

Negotiations Lasted Three Hours with Good Results; Another Meeting Will Be Convened Within Days

According to the Central News Agency, various groups in Shanghai jointly petitioned the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance to provide relief to the market. Yesterday morning at approximately 9:00 AM, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi invited leaders from various sectors to a meeting at the Ministry of Finance office on Rue Mère Amable to discuss relief measures. The meeting lasted three hours and yielded satisfactory results. After individual sectors deliberate separately, another meeting will be convened to discuss implementation methods. Details are as follows:

Attendees: The meeting began at approximately 9:00 AM. Attendees included Kong Xiangxi, Wu Tiecheng, Zou Lin, Chen Xing, Zhang Gongquan, Bei Songsun, Chen Guangfu, Lin Kanghou, Tang Shoumin, Du Yuesheng, Qin Runqing, Guo Shun, Wang Yansong, Yu Zuoting, Yu Qiaqing, Wu Xingya, Cai Zengji, Wu Kaixian, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, and over twenty others, representing various sectors of the Party, government, finance, industry, and commerce.

Objectives of Discussion: The meeting focused on discussing how to alleviate the decline of various current businesses. It was emphasized that each sector should strive to find ways to help itself, while the government should also do its utmost to support the effort. The primary objective was to avoid alarming each other and creating unnecessary panic, and to maintain calm and unity to cope with the situation. It was believed that the current economic situation was not particularly difficult, and that as long as the objectives were clear, people were reassured, and development was jointly planned, the difficulties could be easily resolved.

Another Meeting to Be Held: As a result of the discussions among the leaders, it was agreed in principle that stability and relief were not an issue. However, regarding concrete methods, it was decided that leaders of each sector would be responsible for convening individual meetings to discuss the details. Minister Kong would then convene another meeting to decide on implementation methods. Matters involving other areas were not discussed at the meeting.

Optimistic Outlook: The meeting concluded at 12:30 PM. The representatives felt that the results were satisfactory and were optimistic about the prospects for relief. It was reported that local associations, banking circles, and industrial and commercial sectors were scheduled to convene meetings within the next two days, led by responsible individuals, in order to ensure concerted effort and avoid mutual disruption and stagnation. It was heard that due to the suddenness of the matter, meetings had not been held last night.

Special Committee Meeting: According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the special committee formed by the Shanghai Local Associations to provide relief to the market held a meeting at the Central Trust of China Bank yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. Attendees included Du Yuesheng, Tang Shoumin, Qin Runqing, Bei Songsun, Yu Zuoting, Yu Chenghuan, and others. The meeting lasted until approximately 4:00 PM. According to reporters from the Xin Sheng News Agency, the special committee was studying the issue of providing relief to the market, considering it repeatedly from various perspectives, and planning to implement the previously determined five specific measures. After reporting to Minister Kong, Kong will then convene a meeting to decide on implementation. As for Minister Kong's tea party at his residence yesterday afternoon, it was to entertain foreign guests and was unrelated to providing relief to the market.

The General Labor Union's Standing Committee Met Yesterday to Discuss Ways to Save Industry and Commerce 105

According to the Da Gong News Agency, the Shanghai General Labor Union convened a standing committee meeting yesterday. Committee members Zhu Xuefan, Li Mengnan, Zhou Xuexiang, Long Peiyun, Shao Xubai, Shui Xiangyun, Ye Xianggao, and others were present. Chairman Zhu Xuefan decided on the following three measures: (1) To petition the Central Government to promptly determine fundamental and stop-gap measures for relieving industry and commerce and implement them; (2) To petition the Central Government to instruct manufacturers in all industries to consider the overall situation, to endure the pain and maintain the status quo, and not to hastily cease operations in order to maintain social order; (3) To advise workers throughout the city to share the difficulties, to uphold the spirit of mutual assistance, to cultivate the idea of common survival and prosperity, to work diligently and intensify production, and to protect national industry. Except in cases of extreme necessity, they should not arbitrarily strike or slack off. The above measures were handed over to the Secretariat for prompt handling. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Military Section of the Military Transportation Inspection Group, Including Xu Tingyao, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 107

The Group of Fourteen Arrived in the Afternoon; Will Stay for Two or Three Days Before Reporting to the Capital

According to the Central News Agency, Xu Tingyao, the head of the military section of the Military Transportation Inspection Group, led a group of fourteen members on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso, arriving in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 3:30 PM after travelling from Europe. They will report to the capital within two or three days. The date of their trip to Sichuan to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will be determined after seeking instructions. Xu and his team spent nine months in Europe conducting a thorough examination of the military equipment of various countries. Details of their arrival in Shanghai are as follows:

Arrival Situation: The transportation section of the group, including Yu Feipeng, had arrived in Shanghai on the first of the month, having travelled from America. The military section, since it did not inspect the United States, returned directly from Europe on the Conte Rosso. The ship entered the Wusongkou port at 2:00 PM yesterday and docked at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong at 3:30 PM. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau each sent special boats to welcome the group. Those present included Secretary Tang Shixuan, representing Mayor Wu; Chief of Staff Xu Jinyuan of the Songhu Garrison Command; Wang Zhinan and Wen Hongyin, secretaries of the Municipal Security Office; Cai Jinjun, head of the Municipal Police Bureau; Yu Feipeng, head of the transportation section of the Military Transportation Inspection Group; members Wu Baofeng, Wei Yifu, and Jiang Chuou; Zou Lun, representing Liu Hongsheng, general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company; and dozens of relatives and friends of the group members.

Names of Group Members: The military section of the group consisted of sixteen members. Except for Ji Yongzhong (attached to the Transportation Corps), who remained in Germany to study military communications, and Jiang Chuou, who returned home earlier due to the death of his father, fourteen members returned home yesterday. They were: Xu Tingyao (head), Wang Jinglu, Hua Zhenlin, Si Li, Zheng Fangheng, Tian Gengyuan, Chu Song, Jin Keshao, Ren Runtian, Jia Xuan, Zhang Wen, Xi Wangqing, Zhang Shigang, and Peng Zifang. After landing at the New Customs Wharf, they dispersed to various hotels to rest. Xu, who is about forty years old, wore a black suit yesterday and had a gentle demeanor and the air of a scholar.

Xu's Remarks: According to Xu, who spoke to reporters from various newspapers on board, he and his team were assigned to visit European countries to inspect military equipment, including army organization, military institutions, military industry, military education, etc. They left the country on May 11 of last year. After arriving in Europe, they visited all European countries. Due to time constraints, they did not go to the Americas. Based on their observations, the military equipment of various countries cannot be clearly seen on the surface, so they focused on the development of heavy industry in various countries, as heavy industry is the foundation of military equipment. In any country, if its domestic heavy industry is developed, its military equipment will be impressive. A portion of the inspection report has already been sent back. The reports on Italy and small countries near Italy were sent to Beijing in August of last year. Reports on Germany, Russia, and Czechoslovakia were sent to Beijing in December of last year. Reports on the United Kingdom, France, Sweden, and other countries have been compiled and will be submitted to Beijing in the next two or three days. In addition to this report, a general report will be compiled and refined for reference. The date of the trip to Sichuan to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will be determined after seeking instructions. Xu continued to talk about the international situation, saying that after touring all of Europe, he felt that no country had the determination to go to war. Since the World War, people have been tired of war and chaos. However, the development of various industries in various countries can be used for war at any time, so countries are actively expanding their defense equipment. Taking the United Kingdom as an example, due to its colonial relations, it is actively expanding its military equipment, but its air force equipment is not as good as other countries. The United Kingdom has a population of 45 million, and London accounts for one-fifth of it. Various industries are also concentrated in London, so the British capital is the center of the country's essence. However, its air force equipment is not very thorough. Once an incident occurs, if the enemy air force attacks, it will inevitably suffer great losses. Therefore, the United Kingdom is now actively expanding its air force equipment.

Ministry of Finance Draws Lots for Nine Types of Government Bonds Yesterday Morning 108

A Total of 42 Lots Were Drawn, with Principal Repayments of Over Five Million; The Repayment of the Two-Four Treasury Bills and Other Bills Will Be Made by the End of the Month, 20 Days from Now

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, at the Banking Association Conference Hall on Hong Kong Road, a lottery was held for the repayment of principal on nine types of government bonds, including the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed Two-Four Treasury Bills. More than thirty representatives from various sectors were present. The lottery was chaired by Jiang Lufu, Director of the Government Bond Department. A total of forty-nine lots were drawn, with a total principal repayment of 5,445,000 yuan. All winning bonds, except for the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed Two-Four Treasury Bills, which are scheduled to begin payment on the 20th of this month, the remaining eight types are scheduled to be paid in cash by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various places from the 31st of this month, along with accrued interest. Details are as follows:

Attendees: Jiang Lufu, Director of the Government Bond Department (Chairman); Lin Jinyu, (Inspector) of the Audit Department; Jin Runxiang of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Fan Jietang of the National Debt Fund Management Committee; Tang Shoumin of the Shanghai Banking Association; Liu Wuqiao of the Shanghai Money Exchange Association; (Lottery Drawers) Jin Wenyuan of the Central Bank; Zhu Qizhen of the Bank of China; Shou Rui of the Bank of Communications; (Administrators) He Xiaoyuan, Zong Boxuan, Ran Yaozong; (Recorders) You Dunti, Ji Juncai, Fang Jingzhong; (Document Clerks) Wang Danfen, Huang Qizong, Ling Qixun, Huang Meizhao; (Receptionists) Gong Baozhen, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, Xu Bangzheng; Ju Zhijing of the Shanghai First Special District Court; Luo Qu of the Chinese Securities Exchange; Luo Huizong of the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce; Pan Chuanhe of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; Jin Wenwei of the Shui Bank; Ding Shaoying of the Xiehe Money Exchange; Hua Han of the Guohua Bank; and more than thirty others.

Chairman's Report: Jiang Lufu, Director of the Government Bond Department, reported, stating in brief: Today is the lottery for the repayment of principal on nine types of bonds, including the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed Two-Four Treasury Bills. Except for the 17th Year Financial Long-Term Government Bonds, which, according to the original regulations, repay 1,125,000 yuan each time, and must use a three-digit number lottery method, the remaining eight types of bonds will still use a two-digit number lottery. I will briefly report on the circumstances of each bond: (1) The Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed Two-Four Treasury Bills were issued in 1926 with a total amount of 2.4 million yuan. Sixteen repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 17th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 24,000 yuan. (2) The 7th Year Six District Government Bonds were issued with a total amount of 45 million yuan. Twenty repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 21st repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 450,000 yuan. (3) The 14th Year Government Bonds were issued with a total amount of 15 million yuan. Twenty repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 21st repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 150,000 yuan. (4) The Ministry of Finance Military Needs Government Bonds of the National Government were issued in 1928 with a total amount of 10 million yuan. Sixteen repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 17th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 100,100 yuan. (5) The Ministry of Finance Post-War Short-Term Government Bonds of the National Government were issued in 1928 with a total amount of 40 million yuan. Nineteen repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 20th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 400,000 yuan. (6) The 17th Year Financial Short-Term Government Bonds were issued with a total amount of 30 million yuan. Twelve repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 13th repayment. Ten lots will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 3 million yuan. (7) The 18th Year Disaster Relief Government Bonds were issued with a total amount of 10 million yuan. Eighteen repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 19th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 100,000 yuan. (8) The 19th Year Customs Revenue Government Bonds were issued with a total amount of 20 million yuan. Sixteen repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 17th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 200,500 yuan. (9) The 17th Year Financial Long-Term Government Bonds were issued in 1928 with a total amount of 45 million yuan. Two repayments of principal have already been made. This is the 3rd repayment. Twenty-five lots will be drawn, and the principal repaid will be 1,015,000 yuan. Payments for the above winning bonds, except for the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed Two-Four Treasury Bills, which are scheduled to begin payment on March 20, the remaining eight types of bonds are scheduled to begin payment on March 31. The principal payments for all winning bonds will be made by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various places, along with the accrued interest on each bond. Please have the supervisors check the drawn lots and the bottom slips of the lots so that the lottery can be carried out.

Winning Numbers: After the Chairman's report, the lottery began. Each drawn lot was handed to the supervisor and the chairman for review and announced on a sign. Construction of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway; Land to Be Requisitioned According to Law 109

Announced by the Ministry of Interior

The Ministry of Railways has entrusted the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration with the construction of the railway line from Suzhou to Jiaxing, which is actively underway. The land required for the construction is now being requisitioned by the Ministry of Railways with the approval of the Ministry of Interior according to law. The announcement from the Ministry of Interior is recorded below: "The Ministry of Railways' document (24th Year, Finance, No. 305) states: 'The Suzhou-Jiaxing railway line, passing through Fengmen, Wujiang, Beichi, Pingwang, Shengze, Sanjiangjing, and Jiaxing, is crucial for transportation. The Ministry has ordered the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration to complete the survey. Construction should be actively carried out according to the approved plan, and all land required for the entire line must be requisitioned promptly in order to complete the construction as soon as possible. The Administration has been instructed to comply with the provisions of Article 8 of the Land Requisition Law. The Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway Land Purchase Plan, along with maps, has now been prepared and submitted. We are submitting the documents and maps to you for your review and approval in accordance with the law.' Approved. This is in accordance with the provisions of Article 2, Clause 2 of the Land Requisition Law and should be approved. In addition to replying to your inquiry, please also make a public announcement in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the same law so that everyone is aware. This announcement is made to inform all: (1) The operator of the project is the Ministry of Railways. (2) The type of project is a transportation development project. (3) The area of the project is from the Suzhou Station of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway in Wuxian County, Jiangsu Province, through Wujiang County, to the Jiaxing Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway in Jiaxing County, Zhejiang Province. The total length of the line is approximately 74 kilometers, and the width varies from 42 meters to 200 meters. Approximately 6,800 mu of land will be requisitioned. February 25, 24th Year of the Republic of China."

Silk and Satin Trade Association Passes Commercial Acceptance Bill Procedures 112

Letter requesting Shanghai Silk Industry Bank to promote discounting, sent by the Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Trade Association

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association, in order to improve the credit system and increase currency utilization, created commercial acceptance bills in accordance with the Bills of Exchange Law. After submitting the proposal to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Ninth Executive Supervisory Committee and receiving approval, it sent letters to various businesses, encouraging them to adopt the practice uniformly, and requested that banks and money shops discount the bills as much as possible, and that the Central Bank rediscount them according to law. This was previously reported in this newspaper. It is now understood that this acceptance bill has been studied by the association's chairman for a long time and is considered to be in line with legal principles and actual circumstances. It was unanimously approved at a provisional members' meeting on February 21st of this year and handed over to the association's Executive Supervisory Committee for active implementation. Preparations are now nearing completion. Yesterday, the association held a special standing committee meeting, where Chairman Luo Qinghua reported on the progress of the case and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's reply. The meeting resolved to approve the procedures for using commercial acceptance bills and sent a letter to the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank requesting its promotion and acceptance of discounting to facilitate circulation. Subsequently, Gao Shiheng, a representative of the Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Trade Association, expressed his strong desire to proceed in unison. The usage procedures and correspondence are recorded as follows:

Acceptance Bill Usage Procedures: When customers inquire about payment methods for goods they have selected from this store, aside from cash transactions, there are four types of credit periods: (1) ten days, (2) twenty days, (3) thirty days, and (4) forty days. However, the maximum period should not exceed forty days. The price of the goods should be determined based on the length of the credit period. After the customer specifies the payment date, the price should be negotiated and calculated accurately. Then, the amount of money to be paid and the deadline should be clearly stated on the bill. The credit period is the number of days from the date of sight of the bill until it is due. The customer pays the amount of money listed above. This bill is issued by the seller, who first affixes an official seal. When the goods are delivered to the customer's home, the bill is presented to the customer for acceptance. Upon receiving the bill, the customer should verify the amount and due date. If there are no errors, the customer should affix an official and valid seal under the "Acceptor" section of the bill and return it to the original presenter. The "Presentation Date" on the bill is the date the customer received the bill and affixed their seal of acceptance. The right-hand section of the bill should be cut off by the customer for their records. After the seller receives the accepted bill with the customer's seal, they can sign or stamp the back of the bill and discount it at a bank or money shop to obtain funds for turnover. After receiving the bill, the bank or money shop should first present it to the acceptor for verification. When the bill is due, the acceptor should be asked to affix their original seal again on the blank space on the front of the bill to show their solemnity. On the due date, the holder of the bill (the seller or the bank/money shop) presents the bill to the payment location. The acceptor should immediately pay the full amount. After payment, the acceptor takes back the bill. The holder of the bill does not issue a separate receipt or stamp a return receipt. At this point, the procedures for both parties are complete, and the sales relationship is concluded. After the implementation of this commercial acceptance bill, there are two points that should be clarified. Please ask customers to understand: (1) The amount stated on the bill is the net amount of the transaction and should not be discounted at the time of payment. (2) Payment must be made in cash or immediate bank drafts on the due date to maintain credit. This acceptance bill is issued by the Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association, submitted to the Ninth Executive Committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce for resolution and has been reported to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for approval and record. All members of the trade, whether members or non-members, must purchase from this association at a set price and use it uniformly. Face Format of the Acceptance Bill.

Acceptance Bill Format: The front and back format of the acceptance bill are shown below:

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Reply: We acknowledge receipt of your letter of March 4th, stating that your association is planning to handle commercial acceptance bills to facilitate turnover. You requested that we send letters to various industries to adopt them uniformly, and that we send letters to banks and money shops to discount the aforementioned bills as much as possible, and that we send a special letter to the Central Bank to handle rediscounting. We have investigated the handling of commercial acceptance bills to facilitate turnover, and the Enameled Porcelain industry has once discussed handling it. At a time when funds are insufficient for turnover, it is urgent to promote and imitate. We have already sent letters to various industries, asking them to promote and try it out on their own. As for the extent to which banks and money shops discount and the Central Bank handles rediscounting, this association has this plan in the five rescue measures for the market, and now we have sent a special letter to the Central Bank and banks and money shops to ask them to do so.

Letter to Shanghai Silk Industry Bank: Dear Sirs, We believe that in our country's economic system, in addition to cash, most transactions rely on credit, which delays capital and hinders trade. Now, at a time of industrial and commercial decline and financial exhaustion, we should find ways to improve the credit system as a means of relief. Our industry has always relied on banks and money shops to lend funds to customers for turnover, which has been a long-standing practice. Now that the market is depressed, banks and money shops are tightening lending, resources are exhausted, and economic operations are more difficult than in other industries. If we use cash transactions, we are afraid that it will be difficult to promote in the customer sector because the habit has been entrenched. If we still grant credit, there is no way to attract investment, and we will become more impoverished. In order to plan for the benefit of both buyers and sellers, we have resolved at a temporary members' meeting of our branch to create commercial acceptance bills in accordance with the Bills of Exchange Law, with the aim of reducing the credit period and increasing the use of currency, and we have also sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inform all industries to implement it uniformly. According to the benefits of using commercial acceptance bills, the seller has a definite date for collecting the goods sold in a short time, and can also specially discount them with banks and money shops, so that the currency is increased invisibly, the turnover is flexible, and the business can gradually develop. For the buyer, the payment is fixed on a date so that there is no lack of preparation, and for banks and money shops, this acceptance bill has the joint responsibility of both the issuer and the acceptor, and the term is not too long. If discounting is accepted, it is safer and more reliable than ordinary credit lending. It not only obtains a safe way to invest and profit, but also supports the development of industry and commerce. There is nothing better than to do several good things at once. Moreover, commercial bills have been around for a long time in European and Western countries, and therefore, with the popularity of these bills, the discounting business has also followed suit, and even the establishment of a discounting market has been used as a central hub for operation. Our country is relatively late in adopting the trend, and there will inevitably be difficulties at first in the creation of the aforementioned commercial bills. We know that your bank is a rising star in the banking sector and spares no effort in adjusting finance and serving society, and our silk and satin industry has benefited even more because of its business relationship. Therefore, it has made rapid progress in business and reputation in less than a few years, and it has taken the lead in the trend, created new plans, and planned carefully. Industries and commerce have benefited a lot. Now the commercial acceptance bill created by our industry is the same as your bank's usual purpose, and we hope to invite you to sponsor it. We hope that when our industry implements it on a regular basis, we will allow commercial discounts to circulate, so that both industry and commerce can benefit, not just our industry alone. We sincerely hope for your understanding and a reply.

Recently, the Tobacco and Alcohol Unified Tax Bureau dispatched investigators to repeat the inspection, which is extremely harsh. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to Cai Jinjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting that he forward the consultation to the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to stop sending repeated inspections in order to unify authority and save harshness. The original letter said: We respectfully report that our association has recently received reports from the member pawnshops in the Nanshi district, roughly stating that in addition to the commissioner sent by the Public Security Bureau, the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau also has investigators who come to the pawnshop to conduct the same inspection. When inspecting, they turn over boxes and cabinets and check every detail, which causes great anxiety to merchants. In addition, the Public Security Bureau's commissioner has just finished the inspection, and then the Tax Bureau's investigators come again. Shop assistants are too busy to welcome and send them off, and the business is affected. We hope that the主管官署 (zhuguan guanshu) will be applied to seek correction in order to relieve merchants' difficulties. According to this, we think that the Tax Bureau's levy is originally an inherent power, which cannot be criticized. However, when the authority is not unified, it is easy to cause misunderstandings. Abusing the search will inevitably involve disturbance. In the past, when the Tax Bureau conducted inspections, it was only with the Chamber of Commerce to show solemnity, and the Public Security Bureau only sent police officers to assist. Now, your bureau has established a commissioner to inspect stamps, and the entire inspection responsibility has been assigned. The Tax Bureau does not need to send another investigator. The unified and repeated inspection will inevitably be regarded as true by each party. The situation of the harshness and disturbance of the people is as our members have said. Moreover, which merchant is not willing to affix stamps to all the documents related to the business to prove its validity? Even if there are omissions, it is unintentional. Since there are commissioners who take turns inspecting, the fact is enough to be vigilant. Therefore, our association believes that the Tax Bureau's investigators can be abolished to save public funds and eliminate disturbances. If it is said that the investigators' salaries are meager and rely on the deduction of fines, then the purpose of the inspectors is here and not there, and it is easier to be harsh when performing their duties. At a time when the market is depressed and business is exhausted, if the fault of temporary negligence is suffered from the pain of being summoned for questioning and fined, it is enough to please those who can mention it, and the pain of the merchant's groaning is truly unbearable. This is not the original intention of the national levy. Therefore, the Legislative Yuan has amended the Stamp Tax Ordinance to reduce the punishment as much as possible, which has truly won the hearts of the people. We have long admired your voice and have been concerned about the people's suffering for a long time. The new ideas you have established are admired by all the people. We also ask you to adopt our humble opinion and transfer the document to the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to stop sending repeated inspections in order to unify authority and save harshness. For stamp cases that are detected, those who have omissions or insufficient stamps are unintentional, and we hope to handle them leniently in order to relieve merchants' difficulties. Then, the pawnshop industry will not only feel your kindness. This is above Shanghai Public Security Bureau Director Cai, Shanghai Pawnshop Trade Association.

Shanghai Confucius Youth Association,中華全國道路建設協會 (Zhonghua Quanguo Daolu Jianshe Xiehui) ,中華國貨維持會 (Zhonghua Guohuo Weichi Hui) ,中華航業互助會 (Zhonghua Hangye Huzhu Hui) , Shanghai Citizens Promoting National Goods Association, Zhongshan Shanghai Fellow Association, Shandong Guild Hall, Shanghai Yarn Industry Trade Association, Bean and Rice Trade Association, Copper and Tin Trade Association, Wood Trade Association, Fresh Pig Industry Trade Association, Clock and Watch Industry Trade Association, Egg Industry Trade Association, Frozen Fish Industry Trade Association, and dozens of other groups, with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Mayor Wu making special contributions to the country and local areas, jointly initiated the construction of bronze statues and memorial pavilions in this city to show respect and to encourage future generations. Therefore, the proposal to cast statues has been cancelled, and it is planned to rebuild the Mayor Wu Memorial Pavilion in the city center area in the future to leave a memorial. The construction of a statue of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is still actively underway. He then built the city center area and strived to realize the Greater Shanghai plan. He has made great achievements and is worthy of our worship and respect. New Deli North Sea Sand Ship Encountered Pirates in Qingkou Ocean 118

Pirate ship opened fire to kill crew members, looted cloth worth 20,000 to 30,000 yuan

The New Deli, a North Sea sand boat, set sail on the 1st of this month and headed to Qingkou, at the junction of Jiangsu and Shandong provinces, returning after the fog cleared. It anchored and moored on the shore to avoid the fog. The next morning, as it was weighing anchor, two small boats suddenly sped towards it, firing more than a dozen shots into the sky to stop the ship from sailing. There were more than a dozen pirates on the two boats who used guns to threaten the crew and stop their actions. The captain, Mr. Liu, saw that there were only a dozen pirates and that there were more than 30 crew members on board who could resist. At first, he told the crew to pull up the sail and sail away quickly, but he saw one of the crew members fall to the ground after being shot. He was very frightened and hid in the cabin. Before long, a large three-masted pirate ship arrived, carrying a large gang of pirates. Seeing that there were many pirates, the crew could not risk it and had to stop the ship. The pirates boarded the ship and forced all the crew to stand in one place. The pirates held guns to watch them and searched them one by one. All the silver dollars were looted. They also went to Captain Liu's room to search and smashed open the leather box, looting more than 400 yuan in paper money. After searching, they ordered the ship to sail to the northeast coast of Qingkou to moor. They opened the cabin and forced the crew to carry the goods down to the cabin. Three crew members who were a little late were shot and killed by the pirates. The cloth was loaded onto the large pirate ship and looted for four or five hours. About half of the looted cloth was worth 20,000 to 30,000 yuan. Before leaving, they fired several shots and fled east. After the pirates left, Captain Liu sent the accounts clerk to Shanghai yesterday to report to the merchants who hired the ship, and telegraphed Peng Liji, the shipowner in Nantong, to report the situation of encountering pirates.

Gong and Hou Sentenced to Death for Murdering Xie Aqiao 119

Hou lost her color upon hearing this, her whole body trembling

Gong Shaoting, a Pudong native and owner of the Hongtai Construction Factory on Gongxing Bridge, Zhabei, was already in his sixties. He suddenly lost his wife when he was helping others get married. He was a carpenter and his income was very small. He lacked the funds to remarry, so he became acquainted with Xie Aqiao, a woman from Changshu (Xie Aqiao was an "Ah Ma" in a Westerner's house and had some savings). They rented a house and lived together for nearly 20 years and had always been at peace. Gong was usually very frugal and hard-working. Around 1921, he became a small contractor and his income gradually increased. He operated diligently and his business prospered day by day. He soon founded the Hongtai Construction Factory. Until recently, he accumulated about 100,000 gold. However, Gong Shaoting was inherently stingy and regarded money as his life. He often refused to lend money to relatives and friends, and he would also delay the wages of workers, so the workers were very dissatisfied. Gong became lecherous after getting rich. In the spring of the previous year, he met Mrs. Hou from the Xu family on the road in Caojiadu. They fell in love at first sight and built a new house. A love affair thus began, and a dismemberment tragedy occurred. The trial of this case has been completed by Zhang and Shao, the judges of the local court, and the verdict is pending. Yesterday, at 11:30 a.m., Judge Zhang took the seat in the 10th court and ordered the male and female criminals Gong Shaoting, Hou, Zhou Baoquan, and Li Baosheng, who were in custody, to be brought to the case. He also pre-assigned 10 court police officers to maintain order in the courtroom. The interrogator first briefly asked each criminal about their age and origin, and then stood up and announced the verdict in court. The main text roughly stated that Hou had premeditated murder and was sentenced to death. Damaging the corpse was sentenced to three years in prison. The sentence to be executed was death. Gong Shaoting premeditated murder and was sentenced to 10 years in prison. Inciting abandonment of the corpse was sentenced to five years in prison. The total sentence to be executed was 14 years. Gong Shaoting did not participate in the destruction of the corpse, and the verdict was innocent. In the part of Xie Baolin's request for private prosecution, the verdict was to repay 180 yuan. The remaining requests of Xie Baolin were rejected. Zhou Baoquan and Li Baosheng were sentenced to one year in prison for damaging the corpse. After the interrogator finished the verdict, he said, "If you are not satisfied, you can file an appeal according to law within 10 days." After Gong Shaoting received the verdict, he claimed, "I don't owe him money, so how can you judge me to pay back the money? Of course I am not satisfied." Zhou Baoquan said, "The boss still owes me half a year's salary, totaling 36 yuan." Hou listened to the verdict but did not understand it. She asked the court police who was standing by, "How many years will the old man imprison me for?" The court police replied that she was sentenced to death. Upon hearing the word "death," her face turned pale, her body trembled, and she wanted to cry but had no tears. She greatly regretted it. The interrogator ordered the criminals to be taken away.

Widow Died Strangely After Abortion 120

To save face, a life was lost; The second landlord stole a receipt

Widow Sun Tang, 40 years old, from Gaoyou, lived in the back building of 21 Chunhongfang, Changchun Road, Xingjia Wood Bridge, Zhabei. Her husband had been dead for more than 10 years. After her husband's death, Tang was alone and went out to work as a helper to make a living. Over the past 10 years, she had accumulated some savings. Recently, Tang worked as a helper in the home of a certain family in the French Concession, and became acquainted with a chief steward named Sun Xiaowuzi. They lived together. Unexpectedly, Tang became pregnant, and her abdomen gradually became larger. She thought that if she gave birth, she would lose face, so on the first day of the lunar month, she went to 42 Zhexingli, Xingjiazhai Road, Qiujiang Road, with Sun Xiaowuzi, to eat vegetarian food with Buddhist grandmother Ma Gu (nicknamed Ma Dajie), and asked her to perform an abortion. She did not know that the surgery was not good. After returning home that evening, Tang died tragically at about 1:00 a.m. the next morning. The lover, Sun Xiaowuzi, saw that he had caused trouble, and immediately fled. The second landlord, Qi Songlin, (who lived in the front building) because the deceased still had a cousin, Jin Guoan, who lived at 41, Lane 189, Changchun Road, so he was called to inspect the deceased's belongings. There were two suitcases, 40 pieces of clothing, and 90 yuan in gold circles and paper money, which were taken away by Jin Guoan and his wife for safekeeping. However, it was recently discovered that the second landlord had stolen the deceased's receipt for 200 yuan that was lent to others. Jin Guoan reported to the Sichuan Road Police Station that the cause of Sun Tang's death was unknown. Yesterday, the reporter Jin Guoan, the second landlord Qi Songlin, the guarantor of the deceased's rented house Li Fengshuang, the abortionist Ma Gu who had fled, Gu Xiaoni, Ma Gu's nephew, and the related person Wan Guirong were summoned and questioned. Because the case was complicated and involved criminal cases, it was ruled that Jin Guoan, Qi Songlin, Li Fengshuang, Gu Xiaoni, and Fang Guirong, a total of five people, should be sent to the third section of the Public Security Bureau's Zhabei branch for dispatch.

Xiamen Road: Drug Den Case Opens 121

Chen Zonglian is the Alias of Chen Minghua; Wen Zong'e Faces Additional Charges from the Police

On February 8th of this year, an explosion and collapse occurred at No. 48 and No. 46, Zunde Lane, Xiamen Road, under the name of Xinglong Yufeng, which was in reality a heroin manufacturing den. Besides the deaths of drug-making workers Wang Yongfu and Ji Jinlong, the den's accountant, Tang Jiejun, and workers Wang Yonggui, Gao Guoqing, and Fan Wenxi were also seriously injured. They were arrested by detectives, who also apprehended Wu Guoxian, Gou Hechun, Chen Zonglian, and Wen Zong'e. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday, Qian Hongye, the criminal division chief of the First Special Court, continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, presented the case, stating that the police were prosecuting Tang, Wang, Gao, Fan, Wu, Gou, and Chen under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law, while Wen Zong'e was being prosecuted under Article 216 of the Criminal Law for obstructing freedom and Article 129 for dereliction of duty. Wen, in his position as an inspector for the Jiang-Zhe Consolidated Tax Bureau, allegedly solicited bribes from Chen Zonglian and was involved in the detention of Chen by the Japanese. Therefore, he was being prosecuted in conjunction with the case. However, the lawyer requested that the drug-making case be tried first, followed by the interrogation of Wen on the charges against him. According to the police investigation, Chen Zonglian was the alias of Chen Minghua, the owner of the drug den. However, Chen only admitted to the name Zonglian, styled Zhaozhong, and claimed that Chen Minghua was not himself. The statements of the defendants were then presented to the court. Tang Jiejun confessed that his real name was Tian Jun, styled Jiemin, and that Tang Jiejun was a pseudonym used to avoid embarrassment. He admitted that he was introduced to the job as an accountant in Zunde Lane by the fugitive Li Ziqiang Hejian, and that all his work was completely under the direction of Chen Minghua. When asked in court if Chen Zonglian, who was apprehended, was in fact Chen Minghua, he replied that he was not Chen Minghua. Wang Yonggui, Gao Guoqing, and Fan Wenxi also testified that they were workers and that Chen Zonglian was not Chen Minghua. Wu Guozhi and Xun Hechun both denied any involvement with the drug den. Chen Zonglian testified that he was a counselor in the 26th Division and denied any connection to the drug den. After repeated questioning by the court, Chen firmly denied being Chen Minghua and hired lawyers Jiang Yiping, Fan Gang, and Yu Quncui to defend him. Judge Qian then briefly questioned Wen Zong'e regarding the charges against him. As there was a need for further evidence, the judge ordered a postponement of the trial. Wu Guoxian and Gou Hechun were each granted bail of 2,000 yuan, while the rest were remanded in custody.

Guangxi Woman Sues Post Office Employee for Bigamy 122

Overruled Due to Improper Jurisdiction

Jiang Bingren from Songjiang, an employee of the International Exchange Department of the Shanghai Postal Headquarters, had a physical relationship with Lu Qiongzhen, a young married woman from Laibin County, Guangxi Province, when he was the director of the Liuzhou Post Office in Guangxi two years ago. Later, Jiang was ordered to return to the Shanghai office to take up his current position, thus separating from Lu. Towards the end of last year, Lu suddenly came to Shanghai from Guizhou Province, demanding to reunite with Jiang. She even went to Jiang's hometown for a time before returning to Shanghai. After negotiations, Jiang paid her 200 yuan to return home to avoid her wandering in a foreign land. Lu also wrote a statement declaring a permanent break and promising never to harass him again. Unexpectedly, before the ink was dry, Lu hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation against Jiang Bingren in the First Special District Local Court for bigamy, among other charges. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui opened the court for a preliminary hearing. According to Lu Qiongzhen's testimony, she was 22 years old and married Jiang in Liuzhou on August 5th two years ago. At the time, she was unaware that Jiang had a wife. It was not until she came to Shanghai to visit him on December 29th last year that Jiang took her back to Songjiang the next day, where she learned that he had a wife. She was confined to a small room by his wife and daughters. That night, she seized an opportunity to escape, took a car to Shanghai, and stayed at the Asia Hotel in the French Concession, where she negotiated with Jiang. On January 11th, she signed a permanent separation agreement at the hotel and received 200 yuan. She claimed that Jiang had repeatedly sent people to threaten her, and she needed money for travel expenses, so she accepted the money. Jiang then sent her luggage back through someone, but the clothes in the suitcase had been taken, she said. Jiang Bingren testified that he was 48 years old and had been working in the post office for 22 years. He stated that the plaintiff's allegations were pure fantasy and not worth a laugh. He said that in August two years ago, he was appointed to work in Liuzhou alone. Through the introduction of a local bookseller, he hired the plaintiff as a maid, paying her ten yuan a month. Later, he found her diligent and had an agreement in writing, and then they had a relationship, what is called "za pian tou" (cohabiting) in Shanghai. He never agreed to take her as a concubine. He only gave her 200 yuan out of pity for her impoverished situation to cover her travel expenses. The statement was written voluntarily when she had a moment of conscience, he said. The defendant's lawyer presented the statement and the plaintiff's handwritten letter, arguing that the content of the letter clearly showed the plaintiff's character and that she knew that the defendant had a wife. Judge Liu then told Lu that the fact of the bigamy she was suing for occurred in Liuzhou, the obstruction of freedom and theft occurred in Songjiang, and the forced signing of the statement also occurred in the French Concession. Based on the legal proceedings, the case was not under the jurisdiction of the court. For the convenience of both parties, it would be appropriate to file the lawsuit in the Second Special District Court. After the announcement, the judge dismissed the self-accusation.

Expansion of Municipal Infectious Disease Hospital to Accommodate Nine Statutory Infectious Diseases 123

The Municipal Health Bureau opened the Municipal Infectious Disease Hospital last March at the former site of the Chinese Public Hospital on Tongji Road in Zhabei. The existing wards were not very spacious, so within the possible scope, 64 beds were set up first to temporarily accommodate diphtheria, smallpox, scarlet fever, epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis, cholera, typhus, typhoid fever, and plague, a total of seven infectious diseases. Experts were hired to oversee medical affairs. At the same time, efforts were made to plan for expansion. In July of last summer, construction began on two new, modern infectious disease wards, as well as one office and one clinic. All have now been completed, and the equipment is new and modern, with extremely thorough isolation and disinfection measures. The new and old wards of the entire hospital can now accommodate more than 130 beds. Therefore, starting from March 1st, the scope of treatment will be expanded to fully accommodate nine statutory infectious diseases. In addition to the original seven, typhoid fever and dysentery will be added. In the future, when the economy is more prosperous, wards will continue to be added to achieve perfection. It is reported that the hospital will officially open this month, and invitations will be sent to all sectors to visit.

For the sake of caution, the Social Bureau allows interested parties who have objections to the marriage of the marrying persons to report to the Social Bureau for review before March 28. On the female side, there are 3 at the age of 17, 7 at the age of 18, 3 at the age of 19, 9 at the age of 20, 6 at the age of 21, 6 at the age of 22, 11 at the age of 23, 5 at the age of 24, 2 at the age of 25, 1 at the age of 26, 2 at the age of 27, 1 at the age of 28, 1 at the age of 29, and 1 at the age of 30.

Second Registration Deadline in March

The second group wedding ceremony has been scheduled for May 1 (Wednesday). Registration has already begun and will end on March 11. Those who wish to register may write to the Bureau for an application form and fill it out, along with three full-length 4-inch photos of the man and woman, and a registration fee of 20 yuan. The man and woman must go to the Public Welfare Section of the Bureau to register in person.

Bitter Condemnation of Zhang Damin in Will: Ruan Lingyu Dies with Grievances; Ruan's Body to Lie in State Tomorrow at Funeral Parlor; Young Men and Women Alike Mourn and Pay Respects 127

—Zhang Damin's Case Continues to Be Heard Yesterday—

Since the tragic news of the movie star Ruan Lingyu's suicide was published in newspapers, not only have Ruan's relatives and friends been deeply saddened, but also those who loved Ruan's art have sighed in unison. The following is a compilation of inquiries into the beginning and end of Ruan's suicide:

Transforming into a Vengeful Ghost

Ruan Lingyu was always passionate. After separating from Zhang Damin and officially cohabiting with Tang Jishan, she did not abandon her former relationship with Zhang, still sending him a monthly allowance of one hundred yuan, totaling two years, amounting to two thousand four hundred yuan. Recently, Zhang learned that Ruan was deeply afraid of litigation, and that her position in the film industry was unsuitable for mentioning past events again. To avoid damaging her reputation, he used a lawsuit as a means of coercion, demanding ten thousand yuan from Ruan. Intermediaries negotiated back and forth, and Ruan had already agreed to pay four thousand yuan, but Zhang refused. It was then increased to six thousand yuan, but Zhang still refused. Ruan, feeling that Zhang was excessively oppressive, said indignantly, "He (referring to Zhang Damin) is truly deceiving people too much. Although I am unwilling to confront him in court in this life, I will transform into a vengeful ghost after death to seek retribution!" However, the listeners did not expect that she would immediately contemplate suicide.

Secretly Taking Poison

At about 11 p.m. on the 7th, Ruan was still at the Lianhua Film Studio, chatting with friends and having a late-night snack together. It was not until about 12 a.m. that she returned to the bedroom on the second floor of her residence at No. 9 Qinyuan Village, Xinza Road. At that time, Tang Jishan had already fallen asleep, and Ruan did not disturb him. However, she had talked about the lawsuit with her mother, saying that there was a 99% chance of winning, but she was afraid of being watched by the public in court. Soon after, she claimed to be hungry and ordered the servant to cook a bowl of noodles to satisfy her hunger. Little did anyone know that Ruan had mixed three bottles of Barbitono Sodium sleeping pills, totaling thirty pills, into the noodles and consumed them, resulting in an irredeemable situation. After taking the pills, she also drank two pots of tea.

Obtaining the Pills

Ruan's body was inherently weak. In recent months, she had been working day and night, exhausting herself in her artistic pursuits, and personal misfortunes had continued to plague her, causing severe neurasthenia. She could not fall asleep every night without taking those sleeping pills. There were originally five bottles at home, but Ruan's mother, to avoid any accidents if she lost her mind, had kept them in her possession. In recent days, Ruan had successively devised ways to obtain three bottles of the pills stored by her mother, and eventually used them to end her life. However, it can also be seen that Ruan's determination to die had been made early on, but it had not been known to others.

Final Comfort

After taking the poison, Ruan wrote two wills, one addressed to Tang Jishan and one to all sectors of society (or it is said that one was addressed to Zhang Damin and the other to Tang, but Tang did not allow it to be published. The other is recorded later). After writing them, she hid them in a drawer, then shook Tang awake and asked if he truly loved her. Tang replied that he did indeed truly love her. Ruan then said, "Please give me some comfort (meaning a kiss), because this is the last time." Tang, seeing that her tone and expression were unusual, quickly got up and comforted her, saying, "Why do you say such things? Have you taken poison?" Ruan pretended to laugh and said she had not. Tang did not believe her and called Ruan's mother, who lived on the third floor, to come downstairs. Ruan's mother entered the room, but Ruan was already unable to speak. It was then that they discovered three empty sleeping pill bottles on the table, realizing that she had taken poison. This was about 3 a.m.

No Way to Recover Initially, Ruan had taken poison once and had been sent to the Japanese Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road for treatment and was saved, but that was during the day. This was Ruan's second time taking poison, and the family still followed the same procedure, but they did not know that Fumin Hospital had no doctors on duty at night and that they were somewhat discriminatory against Chinese people. Moreover, it was about 4 a.m. at that time, and it was impossible to find another well-equipped hospital in the northern district. Finally, she was sent to a German doctor surnamed Zhou, and Chen Daming and Chen Jiyao, two brothers who were doctors on Old Bazhi Road, were telegraphed to come for treatment. When they arrived, Ruan was already sleeping on the bed, her makeup still fresh, her slender fingers red with henna, showing no signs of pain. Chen and others immediately used the latest first aid methods, injecting her every fifteen minutes, and performing gastric lavage and enema. She regained consciousness several times, but there was still no hope of survival. She was then sent to the Sino-Western Sanatorium on Pushi Road, using the hospital's ward to perform artificial respiration and oxygen delivery, and immersing Ruan's naked body in a hot water bath, but eventually, due to the delayed rescue, all revival techniques were exhausted, and she breathed her last at 6:38 p.m. on the 8th. According to a doctor, if Ruan had been treated with surgical methods when she arrived at Fumin Hospital, there would have been hope of survival, because at that time the toxicity was still in the stomach and intestines, and had not yet entered the nervous system.

Court Examination

The night before, after the Gordon Road Police Station received a report of Ruan's suicide, they ordered Deputy Inspector Zhu Mengwei and others to investigate, and immediately transported Ruan's body from the Wanguo Funeral Parlor on Jiaozhou Road to the forensic examination office on Feilun Road. At about 10 a.m. yesterday, Song Genshan, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, accompanied by two forensic doctors, Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the office to examine the body. First, the deputy chief of the Western District and others reported the process, and then Tang Jishan stated that he was 41 years old, from Zhongshan County, Guangdong, a tea merchant by trade, and that the deceased was his woman, whom he had formally married. Recently, Zhang Damin had accused him and his wife of adultery and embezzlement, which was actually a false accusation, causing her to suffer this dishonorable matter, resentment, and suicide. Yesterday morning, he returned home and discovered that she was beyond saving, and so on. Ruan He's stated that she was 50 years old, and that the deceased was her daughter. When she committed suicide, she was sleeping upstairs, so she did not know anything beforehand, and now her body was being collected by her husband, Tang Jishan, and so on. After obtaining the statement, Song ruled that the deceased, Ruan Lingyu, was a female who had died of poisoning from an overdose of sleeping pills, and the body was handed over to her husband, Tang Jishan, to collect and coffin it.

Grand Funeral Tomorrow Around 11 a.m., the body was transported back to the Wanguo Funeral Parlor from the examination office. It was then taken to the operating room upstairs for bathing and cosmetic surgery. The date of the grand funeral has been decided for 5 p.m. tomorrow. The obituary has been issued from the Tang residence and sent to Tang and Ruan's friends. The obituary stated that Ms. Ruan was Tang Jishan's wife. In addition to briefly describing the cause of her death, it also stated that the grand funeral would be held at Shen time (3-5 p.m.) on the 11th. Yesterday, Tang's family members were at the funeral parlor preparing for Ruan's final rites. Only Ruan's adopted daughter, Xiaoyu, was inside guarding their residence at No. 9 Qinyuan Village.

Inside the Funeral Parlor

At about 3 p.m. yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency went to the Wanguo Funeral Parlor again to see Ruan's body. At that time, there were many vehicles in front of the door, and there were also many young men and women who were negotiating with the gatekeeper, wanting to go inside to see the body. It was heard that no less than three hundred people had come to pay their respects one after another. Her appearance was even more glamorous than the night before. A dozen flower baskets were placed around the corpse. Underneath, it was hard to resist the feeling of peach blossoms on a human face. Xiaoyu, wearing mourning clothes, was serving beside her mother, with little sorrow, still unaware that this adoptive mother, who had cared for her for several years, was about to part forever. Luo Mingyou, general manager of Lianhua Company, Lin Chuchu, Wang Renmei, Jin Yan, Xu Lai, Xu Qinfang, Liu Jiqun, Yu Guang, photographer Wang Shaofen, dance stars Liang Saizhu and Saisan sisters, Yan Fei, etc., all showed sorrowful expressions. Many of the female stars looked at each other with tears in their eyes. Tang Jishan, wearing a black formal suit, looked dejected, frequently placing flower baskets given by friends and relatives beside Ruan's pillow. Ruan's mother's face was pale, as if she had been crying all day. Everyone was comforting each other. Although Ruan had been separated from this world forever, there were still people who sympathized with her.

Lianhua Telegram

To all newspaper offices across the country, domestic and Nanyang theaters, and readers of Lianhua Films, greetings, Ms. Ruan Lingyu, an actress of our company, suddenly passed away in Shanghai on March 8. All of our colleagues at the company mourn in unison. Please ensure that when your theaters screen Ms. Ruan's works, do not use the unfortunate event of the lady as advertising promotion, so as not to lose the company's consistent pure business and respect for business ethics. Our company's next issue of Lianhua Jin Bao will publish a special memorial issue for Ruan Lingyu. If you have any text to contribute, please send it before March 17. Her last work, "National Customs," has also been completed the day before. The lady's loyalty in serving our company is exemplary. We hope you understand. Respectfully, Lianhua Film Company.

Lianhua Casting a Statue

For the sake of commemorating the lady, all colleagues of Lianhua Company have decided to go to pay their respects in full during the lady's funeral, and hold a memorial service on a regular basis. In addition, the company has decided to raise funds to cast a bronze statue for the lady and place it in the company as a permanent memorial. It has also been decided that the company's colleagues will not send any meaningless elegiac scrolls and flower wreaths, and the money saved will be used for casting the statue. In addition, the film "National Customs," recently starring the lady, has already been filmed. It was recently planned to re-shoot two acts of it, but it is too late. As for the sound film "Spring Comes to the World," which the company was preparing to shoot, it was originally planned to be starred by the lady, and it was about to start shooting, but the lady suddenly became an ancient person.

Two Wills

(1) Now that I am dead, people will surely think that I am afraid of guilt. In fact, what guilt do I have to fear? Because I have never done anything to wrong Zhang Damin. Leaving aside other things, just take the time when I was about to separate from him, I still gave him one hundred yuan every month. This is not just empty talk, there are receipts and vouchers. But he repaid kindness with hatred, and repaid virtue with injustice. What's more, the outside world doesn't understand, and they still think that I have wronged him. Alas, what can I do? After thinking and thinking, the only thing to do is to die. Alas, my death is not a pity, but I am still afraid of gossip. Gossip is terrible. Ruan Lingyu's last words, midnight on the evening of March 7, 24th year of the Republic of China. (2) If I don't die, I can't clear my grievances. Now that I am dead, I can finally fulfill his wishes. Although you did not kill Boren, Boren died because of you. Zhang Damin, I'll see how you escape this public opinion. Now you can't slander Tang Jishan anymore, because you have already killed me.

Trial Opens

Zhang Damin sued Ruan Lingyu, Tang Jishan, etc., for forgery of documents, encroachment, and theft. Although Ms. Ruan Lingyu had committed suicide by taking poison, the Second Special Court still opened the trial at 2 p.m. yesterday. The reason was that the defendant was not only Ruan alone. Since the plaintiff did not withdraw the lawsuit, it would naturally continue. The plaintiff, Zhang Damin, learned of Ruan's death the night before and rushed to the funeral parlor to pay his respects, which caused him to suffer a severe cold, so he was temporarily unable to attend the court for questioning. His attorney appeared on his behalf. The defendant, Tang Jishan, and Ruan's mother, accompanied by their hired defense attorney Jiang Yiping, arrived at the court at about 2 p.m. to report, sitting quietly in the lawyer's lounge waiting for the trial. Tang, who was over fifty years old, looked old and pale, with a short mustache on his upper lip. He was dressed in a Western suit and leather shoes, looking spiritless, due to the excessive stimulation the night before. Ruan's mother, who was about fifty years old, had short hair and wore a black cheongsam, with bound feet and anti-mouth velvet shoes, sitting silently to the side, showing a sorrowful expression. But although Ruan had committed suicide, those who paid attention to the case and went to the court to listen were still very crowded, not diminishing at all, especially women. In the audience seats of the Second Tribunal, there was no space left. The judicial police specially dispatched several policemen to maintain order in the court, which was well-organized. When the bell rang three times, Judge Zhang and the clerk took their seats to hear the case, ordering the court clerk to summon the parties and their attorneys to the case. Tang stood in the defendant's dock. First, the plaintiff's attorney stated that the plaintiff, Zhang Damin, was unable to attend the case today due to excessive cold stimulation, and requested permission to reschedule the date. Questioned by Tang Jishan, who testified that he was 41 years old, from Zhongshan County, Guangdong, residing at No. 9 Qinyuan Village, Avenyi Road, a tea merchant by trade, and had never been criminally punished before. The official said that Ruan Lingyu had committed suicide by taking poison, as reported in the newspaper today. At this point, Jiang Yiping, the defense attorney hired by Ruan and Tang, stood up and declared to the court that after this case occurred, Ruan Lingyu's reputation was greatly damaged in society by the accusations of adultery published in the newspapers, and she was depressed and angry, leading to her suicide by poisoning. In fact, the adultery point was not accurate. Now there are several pieces of evidence and wills that can be submitted to the court for reference. The plaintiff suddenly claimed to be ill today and did not appear, and no evidence was presented, so the request to reschedule the date was unexpected. The plaintiff's attorney said that Ruan Lingyu's suicide, saying that it was caused by being accused of adultery, was just conjecture. Attorney Jiang also stated that Ruan Lingyu and Zhang Damin, in April of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, commissioned Attorney Wu Chengyu to prove and enter into a contract to terminate their cohabitation relationship, which was signed by Zhang in his own handwriting. After the contract was signed, Zhang paid Ruan 100 yuan per month. After the payment of this money ended, this unfortunate case suddenly occurred. Now there is written evidence of the termination of the relationship that can be presented. Jiang also held this evidence in his hand and requested that Attorney Wu be summoned to the case for questioning. Attorney Wu is now in Shanghai, residing on North Sichuan Road, and so on. The official then said to the defendant Tang Jishan, "Since the plaintiff has not arrived today, wait for a scheduled re-summon." He also instructed the defendant's attorney to submit copies of various pieces of evidence to the case at the next hearing. The plaintiff's attorney also stated that although Ruan had died, she had left behind property, which was related to the case of encroachment, and asked whether a disposition could be issued. The defendant Tang Jishan was about to leave Shanghai to do business in Hong Kong, and his whereabouts were uncertain. The court believed that it was necessary to provide bail, and requested that it be properly secured. The court ruled that there was no need to raise it now, and it would be verified at the next trial. The court then adjourned the court.

Fruit Company Resolves Dispute over Dismissal of Warehouse Staff 128

Xieyuan Fruit Company and others, during the Lunar New Year last year, repeatedly used reasons such as poor business and reduced scope, as well as poor performance of warehouse staff, to dismiss many warehouse staff without cause, causing disputes. The warehouse staff who were dismissed included Qian Along of Xieyuan Company, Cai Bingyao of Chengda Company, Xie Guorong and Lu Zhangfu of Huitai Company, Weng Jiancheng, Yan Xinlong, and Song Tulin of Yongxing Company, Yu Kunyu and Luo Gentu of Taifeng Company, Xiang Asi and Lu Afu of Jicheng Company, etc. They immediately reported to the Fruit Industry Warehouse Staff Association, requesting a transfer report, and the dismissed workers themselves petitioned the party and government agencies for relief. The association immediately transferred the report according to the situation, requesting that the relevant companies be ordered to reinstate all the dismissed warehouse staff to avoid disputes and maintain the difficult situation. At the same time, staff were sent to consult with the managers of the various companies, requesting reinstatement. The managers of Chengda, Huitai, Yongyu, Taifeng, Fucheng, and other companies, after considering the difficult livelihood of the warehouse staff and their special nature, and in accordance with the Municipal Party Department's Notice No. 203, published in newspapers, notifying all industrial and commercial firms not to dismiss workers without cause during the settlement period, so as not to cause disputes, especially reinstating all the dismissed warehouse staff of the relevant companies. The Fruit Industry Warehouse Staff Association and all its members expressed their deep gratitude to the companies that agreed to reinstate them. However, Xu Runsheng, the manager of Xieyuan Company, although repeatedly persuaded and mediated by Commissioner Lu (Jingshi) of the Municipal Party Department, and the Fruit Industry Warehouse Staff Association repeatedly sent staff to consult, was ultimately stubborn and resistant. In order to settle the matter, the labor side followed Commissioner Lu's instructions: (1) Issuing Qian Along with 30 yuan for travel expenses, waiting for work; (2) If there is a vacancy in the future, Qian Along must be given priority to work. It is heard that the labor side's method was purely to follow the Party Department's mediation intentions, receiving money was not their original intention, so they immediately sent the money received to the Shanghai Fundraising Committee for Drought Relief in Various Provinces to relieve the victims. The dispute has been temporarily settled.

Rickshaw Pullers Demand Return of Confiscated Vehicle Licenses 129

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Public Concession Bureau's Rickshaw Affairs Committee confiscated ten licenses and suspended their issuance for half a month and one month due to rickshaw pullers overcharging fares. However, the rickshaw pullers said that they had previously contacted the Vehicle Committee, and in addition to the fare of eight jiao and five fen, they could also charge for the rickshaw puller's meals and rental deposit. Now the Vehicle Committee disregards everything, confiscates the licenses and does not allow them to operate. Therefore, the rickshaw pullers whose licenses have been confiscated have jointly sent a letter to the guild, requesting that they negotiate with the Vehicle Committee to return them.
