Party, Government, and Military Representatives Publicly Commemorate Chen Shaobai Yesterday 130

Wu Tiecheng Presides, Tong Xingbai and Others Accompany; After the Ceremony, the Remains Are Sent to the Haili Wheel for Transportation to Guangdong for Public Burial

The coffin of Mr. Chen Shaobai, a pioneer of the Party and the country, was transported back to Guangdong by Pingyun. On the morning of the 8th, it passed through the capital, and central figures held a public memorial service in Xiaguan. At noon on the same day, it was attached to the Beijing-Shanghai fourth train and transported to the North Station of this city. The municipal government sent Zhou Guoping to take care of everything. Party, government, and military circles of this city held a public memorial service in front of the coffin flower car at the North Station at 9 a.m. yesterday. At 10 a.m., a coffin transport car was used to transfer it to Jinliyuan Wharf, where it was loaded onto the Haili Wheel, which set sail at 2 p.m. to transport it back to its hometown. The details are recorded as follows:

Dispatching Police Protection Chen's coffin flower car was parked at the Songhu branch line of the North Station. A public memorial altar was set up in front of the car. A portrait of Mr. Chen Shaobai was hung on the altar, with fruits offered and candles lit and incense burned. Flower wreaths sent by various circles surrounded it. At the entrance, there was a plain-colored archway made of silk. The military band dispatched by the Municipal Public Security Bureau stood to the right of the altar, and additional police officers were dispatched to stand around to provide protection. The situation was very solemn.

Participating Figures Among those who participated in the public memorial service were Mayor Wu, Tong Xingbai, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Department, Jiang Huaisu, Secretary-General, Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Yang Xiaotian, Director of the Security Office, Li Dachao, Chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government, Wu Shaohui, Deputy Director of the Two-Road Administration Bureau, Xu Yuanfang, Director of the General Affairs Office, Qiao Yisheng of the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai Office, Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University, and other hundred people. Mayor Wu presided over the ceremony, Lin Yannan was the master of ceremonies, Zhou Tongping was the host, and Chen Tongjia read the memorial text.

Public Memorial Situation After Mayor Wu arrived at the venue, he expressed his condolences to the Chen family and began the public memorial service. Mayor Wu, the presiding officer, and Tong Xingbai, Jiang Aosu, Yang Xiaotian, and others, the accompanying officers, stood in front of the altar in order, facing the altar. The family members stood on the right side of the altar. The master of ceremonies stood on the left side, and the reader of the memorial text also stood on the right side. First, the military band of the Municipal Public Security Bureau played funeral music, and the whole body bowed three times to the portrait of Mr. Chen Shaobai. Then, the presiding officer presented a wreath, burned incense, and remained silent. Then, the reader of the memorial text read the memorial text, and the whole body bowed once to the family members. The family members returned the bow, and the ceremony was announced as complete. After the public memorial ceremony was completed, Mayor Wu and others boarded the car to view the coffin. The coffin was covered with flower wreaths and had a portrait of Mr. Chen Shaobai hanging on it. The family members, including Mrs. Chen, accompanied him on the side. Mayor Wu inquired about the situation of transporting the coffin back to his hometown, and the family members answered in detail. Mayor Wu, with other important matters to attend to, took his leave first and changed to a car to go to the Kong residence on West Aimes Road.

Party and Government Memorial Text On the ninth day of March in the twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China, Wu Tiecheng and others, the representatives of the Shanghai municipal party, government, and military, respectfully offer incense, flowers, wine, and sacrifices to the spirit of Mr. Shaobai, saying, "In ancient times, sages and wise men, men of great talent, who intended to accomplish great things in the world, must have had outstanding heroes and heroines assisting and supporting them, planning and strategizing in the command tent, borrowing chopsticks at the side of the ash pan, so that they complemented each other and their merits became more obvious. Yao's relationship with the Four Mountains, Shun's relationship with Yuankai, Tang's relationship with Yi Yin, and Zhou's relationship with Lu Shang, all recorded in historical records, were all like this. As for those who pursue righteousness and do not admire profit, work diligently and do not count their merits, there has never been anyone like you, sir. In the beginning, Xiao He transported grain to Guanzhong, and ultimately revived the Han Dynasty. In the end, Yan Guang resided in the rocky mountains, and even moved the heavenly stars. Li Bi still held the position of Yuanfu, and Zhang Liang ultimately received the reward of Marquis Liu. Sir, your righteousness was deep in friendship, you dedicated yourself to the revolution, your heart was as firm as gold and stone, you personally braved dangers and ran around the seas and skies, secretly planning and raising arms and equipment for thirty years as if it were one day. The Premier regarded you as a teacher and friend, and the Party and the country revered you as a pioneer. Yet you did not speak of your merits and did not accept rewards. After the revolution was completed, you retired cleanly, which can be said to combine Zifang and Ziling into one person, and even surpass them. After the Premier passed away, your contemporaries also withered away. Only you, sir, with a scattered body, leisurely enjoyed the forests and streams, hoping that you could enjoy a long life, and stand巍然as the Lu Temple Lingguang. Then, the bad news came, the old and accomplished passed away, the whole country was shocked and mourned, and the whole world was in mourning. In your case, sir, you rode on Jiwei and traveled in the vastness of the universe. Your bright integrity and noble demeanor are recorded in historical records. The central government has the canon of commendation, and your hometown has the grand funeral rites, which are extremely honorable and leave no regrets. However, in this time of national crisis, we rely on the model of the advanced as a model for the people. The passing of a man is a national bereavement. Now, the Danliu returns south, and the spirit chariot passes through Shanghai. Tiecheng and others bear the responsibility of defending the land, obey the orders of the central government, remember the predecessors, admire the high virtues, and both public and private feelings are intertwined. Seeing the posthumous appearance, we shed tears. Touching the coffin, we swallow our voices. If the gods have spirits, we hope that they will come and be present. Alas, may you enjoy the sacrifice."

Transport to Guangdong for Public Burial At about 10 a.m., Chen's coffin was transferred from the coffin flower car to the coffin transport car and driven to Jinliyuan Wharf. Representatives from various circles sent him off at the rear, and the military band of the Municipal Public Security Bureau also accompanied him. After arriving at Jinliyuan Wharf, Chen's coffin was transferred to the Haili Wheel of the China Merchants Bureau. At that time, the military band played funeral music, and family members also boarded the ship. At 2 p.m., the Haili Wheel set sail and left Shanghai, transporting it back to its hometown. Chen's friends then bid farewell to Chen's family.

Representative of the Industry and Commerce Relief Association to Petition Kong, Soong, et al. Tomorrow 131

Five representatives, including Chen Xiaodie and Jin Runxiang, designated; to host a press reception at the Central Western Restaurant tonight.

According to the New Voice Society, the Shanghai Chinese Industry and Commerce Relief Association held a board meeting the night before last at 8 PM. Representatives were designated to petition Finance Minister Kong and others tomorrow. A press reception will be held today. Details are as follows:

Board Meeting

At 8 PM the night before last, the association held a meeting of all board members at its headquarters. Twenty-four members attended, chaired by Chen Xiaodie and recorded by Cao Zhigong. The following resolutions were reached after discussion: (1) Regarding the publication of a declaration: (Resolved) To publish an advertisement in major newspapers on the 10th. (2) Regarding the petition to the authorities for relief: (Resolved) To send Chen Xiaodie, Hong Yanbin, Wu Zhihao, Zhang Rongchu, and four others to petition Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, National Economic Committee Standing Committee member Soong Ziwen, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and the Municipal Party Headquarters, Social Bureau, and five other agencies at 9 AM on the 11th. (3) Review of methods for relieving industry and commerce: (Resolved) To assign Chen Xiaodie, Jin Runxiang, Hong Yanbin, Ren Jinpin, Qin Daishi, Shen Tianxin, and Wu Zhigao, along with the original drafters, to review fundamental solutions for relieving industry and commerce. (4) Regarding the additional appointment of Xue Mingjian, Xu Jutang, Cheng Shouzhong, Shen Tianxin, Li Weiliang, Cheng Zhu, Qu Zhenhua, Sheng, Wang Binyan, Sun Daosheng, and Ren Jinpin as directors of the association: (Resolved) Passed. (5) Regarding the scheduling of a press reception for publicity and liaison purposes: (Resolved) To hold it at the Central Western Restaurant at 6 PM on the 10th. (6) Regarding the additional appointment of Hu Fengxiang, Zhu Xuefan, and Shao Xubai as standing directors. (7) Regarding the revision of the association's charter: (Resolved) Passed.

Revised Charter

(Article 1) The association's purpose is to provide relief to Chinese industry and commerce, and it is named the Chinese Industry and Commerce Relief Association. (Article 2) Any individual or organization that agrees with the association's purpose may be admitted as a member upon the recommendation of two or more founding members and approval by the Standing Committee. (Article 3) The association's expenses shall be borne by the members, and are divided into the following two items: (1) Membership fee of one yuan. (2) Special donations will be contributed by each member according to their ability. (Article 4) The association shall be governed by a board of directors consisting of thirty-five to forty-five members elected by the members. (Article 5) The board of directors shall elect nine to fifteen standing directors to handle daily affairs. (Article 6) The board of directors shall establish five groups: General Affairs, Economy, Design, Organization, and Investigation. Each group shall have one director and one deputy director, elected from among the directors. (Article 7) Each group may have a number of committee members, determined by the complexity of the affairs, appointed by the group director upon approval by the board of directors. (Article 8) The board of directors shall establish a secretariat with two to four secretaries to handle daily affairs under the direction of the standing committee. (Article 9) The secretariat shall be divided into three sections: Documentation, Accounting, and General Affairs. Each section shall have a director to manage its affairs. (Article 10) The number of staff in each section shall be determined by the complexity of the affairs. (Article 11) When necessary, secretaries and staff may receive transportation allowances, the amount of which shall be determined by the Standing Committee. (Article 12) The Standing Committee shall meet every three days, and special meetings may be convened with the consent of two or more Standing Committee members when necessary. (Article 13) The board of directors shall meet once a week, and special meetings may be convened by the Standing Committee when necessary. (Article 14) All meetings of the association require a quorum of more than half of the members to be convened, and a majority vote of those present is required for a resolution to be passed. In the event of a tie, the decision shall be made by the chair. (Article 15) When necessary, the association may establish specialized committees, with experts appointed by the Standing Committee. (Article 16) Detailed rules for the association's operations shall be determined separately. (Article 17) These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the founding members. Any matters not covered shall be amended by a vote of the general membership.

Hepburn and Ormond Barlow to visit Tang Xifen today to discuss selection and transport.

To celebrate the 25th anniversary of the coronation of the British Emperor, the British government has specifically requested that valuable antiquities be transported from our country to be held in London at an international art exhibition. The British government attaches great importance to this event and has sent special commissioners to China to assist. Veit and Raphael have already arrived. Hepburn and Ormond Barlow will arrive tomorrow morning. Hepburn and Ormond both hold positions at the British Royal Museum and have extensive knowledge of oriental antiquities. Hepburn and Ormond are scheduled to visit Tang Xifen, the secretary of our organizing committee, today to discuss the selection and transport of antiquities to England. Chinese Muslims to Return Home After Completing Pilgrimage 135

Expected to arrive in Shanghai on May 14th

Fire on Tram in French Concession 136

Tram No. 42, Route 7, operated by the French Tram Company, traveling from the Sixteen Arches to Rue Massenet, suddenly emitted smoke and fire from its undercarriage at 4:10 PM yesterday when it reached the tram stop in front of the police station at Avenue Dubail and Rue de Montauban. The car was filled with smoke, and the ticket seller urgently instructed all passengers to disembark. He then quickly shut off the engine. The smoke and fire were caused by the motor pulley overheating, which ignited the undercarriage. Upon hearing the alarm, firefighters rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire, and the police dispatched officers to control the crowd around the burning tram. As a result, trams traveling east and west were blocked and unable to move forward, from Rue McGibbon all the way to the fire station on Avenue Dubail, numbering more than a dozen, like a long snake. It took about half an hour for the firefighters to extinguish the fire under the tram and restore traffic. However, when the tram undercarriage emitted smoke and fire, all the passengers were greatly frightened.

Yesterday's Jiangda Basketball Game: Fudan Wins Big Against Chihchih 145

98 to 18, a new record for the season. Jinan defeats Guanglu with 69 to 19

In yesterday's Jiangda basketball game, Fudan played against Chihchih at the Fudan Gymnasium. About five or six hundred spectators were in attendance, crowding together and cheering from time to time. Fudan was last year's champion and has strong strength. Chihchih has many new players whose skills are still lacking. The game looked like an egg hitting a stone. As a result, Fudan won a great victory with a score of 98 to 18. The magnitude of the score can be described as a new record for the season.

Disparity in Strength

After the referee blew the whistle to start the game, Fudan's Chuan Xiangfu immediately scored three consecutive goals. Chihchih suddenly appeared flustered and helpless, unable to attack and unable to defend. The situation deteriorated rapidly. Chihchih only scored two points from a long shot by its defender Lu Zhixin and managed nothing else. As a result, the first half ended with a score of 55 to 4.

Difficult to Reverse the Tide After the lemon break, Fudan's Ma Kaihua came on and replaced Shen Chongjiao, and the competition became slightly more interesting. However, Chihchih's forwards were inaccurate in their shots, making it impossible to reverse the already reversed tide. Fudan's players scored every time they shot. When the whistle blew, Fudan achieved a great victory with a score of 98 to 18.

Tung Wah Still Virgin, Yu You Suffers Another Crushing Defeat with 1 to 4. Both Sides Exhibited Harmony, with Clear and Watchable Moves. The Tung Wah First Division Championship Is Secure. 146

Luo Hua and Yu You met again in Yi Yuan on the afternoon of the day for the second round of the Western Football First Division League. Due to the absence of one or two key players, Yu You's offensive strength was weakened. As a result, Tung Wah won 4 to 1, creating a record of 10 wins in the First Division. Yesterday, the weather was mild, the sun was shining, and the spring air was full of joy. There were as many as three or four thousand men and women in red and green in Yi Yuan Stadium. The performance of both sides was clear, and the fans were very satisfied.

Zhang Rongcai's Goalkeeping Was Excellent

Victory and defeat are common in military affairs. Sports must emphasize spirit. The performance of Tung Wah and Yu You yesterday can be described as the ultimate in courtesy. As for offensive and defensive operations, they each did their best without any laziness. That is where the spirit lies. Yu You's defense was better than its offense yesterday. Zhang Rongcai's goalkeeping was highly praised. Given time, he will definitely be impressive. Chen Zhenxiang also stood out from his peers. Forward Sun Jinshun was unable to accomplish much alone. Tung Wah's victory was entirely due to the better cooperation of its forwards. The defense was similar, but the offense won. Jia Youliang moved like the wind and was the most energetic. Among the five forwards, Qin Zuo Zhi was the most average because he was inexperienced.

Stalemate Lasted for 40 Minutes

Yu You kicked off. In the first ten minutes, the chances for both sides were very equal. There was offense and defense, with each side gaining and losing. Yu You's Chen Zhenxiang performed outstandingly. Gradually, Tung Wah began to dominate the offense. However, because Qin Zuozhi's movements were too slow, he simply watched the opportunities and sighed. Yu You's Zhong Yongsen also exchanged positions with Liu Zuxiu, making the situation slightly better. Zhang Rongcai was in the limelight. Tung Wah's attacks, which could have scored three times, were all stopped by Zhang. Jia Youliang's shot at the goal was extremely powerful but was also saved by Zhang. Cheers erupted for a time.

Chen Jiaqiu Unleashed a Cold Arrow

The stalemate lasted until the last two minutes of the first half. Qin Zuozhi got the ball in the left corner. Tung Wah's five forwards rushed forward. Qin passed to the front of the goal. After Dai Linjing got the ball, he passed it to Chen Jiaqiu, who lifted his foot behind the crowd and sent a high ball that happened to fall into the goal. Zhang Rongcai jumped up to catch the ball, but it had already fallen into the net. Tung Wah opened the scoring first. Turning around to kick off in the center, the whistle blew for the break. Tung Wah was ahead by one goal to zero in the first half.

Li Dai Scored Three More Goals

Switching sides to fight again, Yu You used all its strength and made efforts to improve. However, the forwards lacked coordination and were often intercepted halfway. Tung Wah then launched a fierce attack. Qin Zuozhi took a corner kick and lingered in front of the goal. Li Yichen broke through the encirclement and shot powerfully at the goal. The ball hit the corner of the net. In less than two minutes, Jia Youliang selected the center. A Dai took advantage of the opportunity to attack and scored, leaving the goalkeeper with no way to stop it. After a while, Dai got a pass from Qin and scored another goal, making it three goals and a clean four goals.

Sun Jinshun Scored a Goal Back

Tung Wah, without losing a single soldier, scored four consecutive goals, its momentum soaring and its light shining. Yu You's entire army was indignant and determined to retaliate. Sun Jinshun broke through the crowd and crossed two hurdles. When he reached a suitable spot, he waved his iron leg and flew the ball into the net, regaining one goal. Before long, time was up. Although Yu You wanted to counterattack, it could not. Tung Wah won with four goals to one.

Education News

Ministry of Education Guidance: Methods for Schools in Various Regions to Study Educational Issues (2) 154

Issues that elementary education research conferences at all levels should study in the near future (proposed by the Ministry of Education)

A. Regarding Curriculum

(1) Should the subjects and time allocation of the current elementary school curriculum be changed? (1) What subjects can be removed or reduced in primary schools, and how should they be reduced? (2) What subjects can be combined? (3) Should the total time be appropriately reduced? (4) Should the teaching hours of which subjects be reduced or increased?

(2) What are the shortcomings and difficulties in implementing the current elementary school curriculum, and how can they be remedied?

(3) Should the content of the current elementary school Chinese textbooks be changed? (1) Are stories unusable, or are there too many? (2) Should children's literature be the center, or should various knowledge be introduced to children through Chinese? (3) What conditions should the most ideal Chinese textbook meet?

B. Regarding Teaching

(1) How to avoid wasting time in teaching and make teaching work intense?

(2) How to examine children's academic performance?

(3) How to examine children's performance in civic training?

(4) How to pay attention to physical education and hygiene to improve children's physical health?

C. Regarding Equipment

(1) What is the most economical and suitable school building style, and how should it be built?

(2) What school equipment, teaching aids, and forms should elementary schools have at a minimum?

D. Regarding Educational Administration

(1) Should examinations similar to joint entrance examinations be held at elementary school graduation?

(2) What are your opinions on the current elementary school regulations?

(3) How to assist in promoting compulsory education?

Practical Issues and Examples for Studying Secondary School and Normal School Education

1. Curriculum

(1) Research on the issue of whether the subjects and time allocation in the secondary school curriculum should be reduced. (1) Should the subjects and the total weekly hours be appropriately reduced? (2) Which subjects should be reduced? (3) How many weekly hours should be reduced? (4) How many hours should the hours of a certain subject be increased or decreased? (5) How should Tables 1 and 2 of the weekly teaching and self-study hours in secondary schools be redistributed?

(2) Research on whether the time and content of mathematics in secondary schools should be changed. 1. Should mathematics in secondary schools be divided into groups? 2. Should the time allocation and syllabus of the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry be changed? Attached is the proposal for revising the secondary school mathematics curriculum standards by Mr. Mei Yiqi and others for reference.

2. Teachers

(1) Opinions on the Interim Regulations for the Examination of Teachers in Secondary Schools and Normal Schools.

(2) Suggestions on improving teacher training institutions in secondary schools.

(3) How should teachers in secondary schools and normal schools pursue further education?

3. Graduation Joint Entrance Examination

(1) Should school graduation examinations be abolished?

(2) If students who fail one or two subjects in senior high school fail the re-examination twice but have been admitted to colleges or universities for trial study, how should the issue of their academic status be resolved?

(3) Should normal school students who fail one or two subjects in the graduation examination be allowed to serve temporarily first?

(4) Should the calculation and disclosure methods of the joint entrance examination results in schools be changed?

4. Equipment

(1) How can the equipment for natural sciences in secondary schools and normal schools be improved?

(2) Opinions on equipment standards.

(3) What percentage of the total school expenses should be allocated to teaching equipment expenses?

5. Funding

(1) Opinions on the Ministry's funding allocation standards.

(2) How to reform the forgery of bills and the bad practices of stores so that every penny goes to the public?

6. Moral Education and Military Management

(1) Opinions on defining the content of moral education standards.

(2) How to ensure that school moral education is instilled into every student's actual life?

(3) What difficulties are there in student management after centralized military training is implemented?

(4) Suggestions on the implementation methods of military management.

Ministry of Education: Interpretation of the Compilation of Educational Laws and Regulations 155

The Ministry of Education has recently issued several interpretations of educational laws and regulations, which are summarized below: A. Regarding matters related to secondary school joint entrance examinations: (1) The Ministry of Education ordered the Hebei Education Department (regarding how to handle students who failed one or two subjects in the senior high school graduation joint entrance examination and have already been admitted to universities, and whether they can transfer schools during the trial study period), stating that students who failed one or two subjects in the senior high school joint entrance examination should be allowed to participate in the re-examination of the failed subjects for a maximum of two times. If they still fail, they should be ordered to withdraw from school. As for transferring schools, it should be approved only after they become official students. (2) To explain the standards for calculating the results of schools participating in the graduation joint entrance examination, the Ministry of Education ordered the Yi Education Department, stating that secondary schools with both senior and junior high school classes should list their senior high school students in the same list as other senior high schools, and their junior high school students in a separate list as other junior high schools. The three proportions stipulated in Article 12 of the joint entrance examination regulations should be calculated separately according to the regulations to determine the percentages of grades A, B, C, and D. (3) To explain the ambiguity in Article 10 of the Secondary School Student Graduation Joint Entrance Examination Regulations, the Ministry of Education consulted the Guizhou Provincial Government (details omitted). Students who fail one or two subjects in the graduation joint entrance examination should be allowed to participate in the re-examination of the failed subjects for a maximum of two times. Those who cannot participate in the re-examination due to unavoidable reasons may be issued a certificate of completion by the original school, stating the grades of each subject in the joint entrance examination and indicating the subjects that were failed. In addition, if the above-mentioned students who failed have already gone to school outside the province, the original education department may entrust the education department or bureau of the province where they are currently studying to conduct a re-examination on their behalf. B. The Vocational Supplementary School Regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education are different from the Merchant Supplementary School Regulations promulgated by the Central People's Movement Committee. The Ministry of Education ordered the Zhejiang Education Department, stating that Article 1 of the Vocational Supplementary School Regulations stipulates that the purpose of vocational supplementary schools is to provide those who are already engaged in or aspire to engage in a certain occupation with knowledge and skills in that occupation. Its sub-discipline methods and curriculum content are different from the general supplementary schools mentioned in the key points of the Merchant Supplementary School Regulations. If various groups or individuals want to establish the aforementioned vocational supplementary schools, they should still refer to the Vocational Supplementary School Regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education.

C. To explain the qualifications of graduates of one-year normal courses and graduates of public and private secondary schools before the Qing Dynasty or before 1927, the Ministry of Education ordered the Jiangsu Education Department, stating that the following is hereby approved after review: (1) Graduates of one-year normal courses who have served as elementary school teachers for more than one year may be exempted from examination and verification in accordance with Article 78, Paragraph 2 of the Elementary School Regulations. (2) The qualifications of graduates of public secondary schools before 1927 or the Qing Dynasty may be uniformly recognized. However, the recognition of the qualifications of students from private secondary schools registered by the former Beijing Ministry of Education should be handled in accordance with Announcement No. 9 of the Ministry in 1930. The Jiangnan Arsenal Vocational School is a military school, which is different from ordinary schools. Its graduates cannot be exempted from examination for ordinary elementary school teachers.

The National Academic Work Advisory Office Hosted the Press Yesterday 158

Director Cheng Zhenji Reported on the General Situation of the Work

—The Employment Guidance Committee Also Held an Inaugural Meeting at the Same Time—

—Important Cases Were Discussed and He Qingru Was Elected as a Standing Committee Member—

The National Academic Work Advisory Office, a national talent coordination agency, has been established for five months. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the office held the inaugural meeting of the Employment Guidance Committee on the ninth floor of the Shanghai YMCA, and at 4:00 PM, hosted the Shanghai press at the same location to report on the general situation of the work. The details are recorded as follows:

(1) Establishment of the Employment Guidance Committee

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the National Academic Work Advisory Office held the inaugural meeting of the Employment Guidance Committee on the ninth floor of the Shanghai YMCA, and the first meeting. Those who attended included Cheng Zhenji, director of the office, Yu Tongkui, deputy director, Zhao Enju, secretary, Li Zhaohuan, president of Jiaotong University, Liu Zhanen, president of Shanghai University, Pan Yangyao from the Vocational Guidance Institute, Jiang Wenyu (represented by Yang Chongfu) from the Vocational Education Society, He Qingru, Ou Yuanhuai, president of Daxia University, Cao Yunxiang, Ye Gongchuo, Dai Zhiqian, Wang Zhixin, etc. He Qingru was the chairman, and Zhao Enju was the secretary. Reporting items included: (1) The Advisory Office introduced the employment situation. (2) Liaison methods with domestic and foreign employment agencies.

Resolutions: (1) Revising and passing the rules of procedure for this meeting. (2) Deciding whether this committee should set up an office in Shanghai. It was decided that the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute would be the liaison office of this committee. (3) There are thousands of employment introduction matters. If there is no fixed guideline, it will inevitably take a lot of effort but achieve little results. How should the introduction work be carried out in the future? (4) Unemployment of academic personnel is a common phenomenon in China. Due to limited funding, this office cannot widely establish branch offices, so the introduction work has not been popularized throughout the country. How should we contact and promote domestic and foreign employment agencies? (5) The main task of this office is to coordinate talents so that both supply and demand have appropriate contact. However, in a scattered and chaotic situation, how should this task be carried out to achieve results? It was decided that the above three items would be handled together. A. This office should first contact and liaise with various administrative agencies and local trade associations, and ask them to give priority to employing the academic personnel introduced by this office. B. This office should urge schools above the specialized level that have not organized employment agencies to establish them as soon as possible, and conduct a detailed survey of the employment status of graduates of each school, compile statistics and reports, and provide appropriate introductions. (6) Temporary motion. Committee member Dai proposed to establish one standing committee member. It was decided to elect He Qingru to serve as the standing committee member. The meeting adjourned.

He Qingru Talks. A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency asked Dr. He Qingru, a standing committee member of the committee, about the future work direction of the Employment Guidance Committee. According to him, various methods will be adopted, starting from multiple aspects, to promote and expand the introduction work of the Advisory Office, so as to make all parties have a clear understanding of the Advisory Office, and facilitate assistance and development, to achieve the ultimate goal of talent coordination.

(2) Situation of Hosting the Press

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the office hosted the Shanghai press at the same location. More than 30 people from various newspapers, including Ma Chonggan, Xia Kaiming, Zhu Zhiwu, Yu Jinkang, Zhu Zhongzheng, Hu Hanjun, Zhou Tianqiu, Xue Wubing, Wang Jinqi, and Yu Jiawei, attended. Yang Chongfu and others hosted the event. After refreshments, Cheng Zhenji, director of the office, first reported on the significance of the Advisory Office and the general situation of the work. Deputy Director Yu Tongkui continued to report. Finally, Ma Chonggan and others made speeches. The event ended at around 6:00 PM.

Cheng's Report. Cheng Zhenji, chairman of the National Academic Work Advisory Office, reported on the general situation, saying, "I am very happy to be able to gather with you today. The office has only been established for five months, and the organization is very simple, but the cause is in its infancy and lacks guidelines. Most of the colleagues in the office have no experience in this work, so omissions and errors are inevitable. However, we can only bury our heads and work hard. Today, I would like to take this opportunity to briefly report to you on the meaning of the establishment of this office and the general situation of the work in the past five months. I hope you will give us more advice."

Purpose of Establishment. "This office is a talent coordination agency jointly established by the National Economic Commission and the Ministry of Education. The purpose is to make the supply and demand of academic talents in the country have appropriate contact, so as to achieve the effect of 'getting the right person for the job and the right job for the person.' The country's construction requires talent urgently, and the authorities often have difficulty finding talent, while academic personnel cannot find jobs, and some are under economic pressure and have to choose jobs that are not suitable for them. Based on this understanding, the government established this office to coordinate and promulgated regulations as the basis for handling affairs."

Internal Work. "This office follows the internal work defined by the regulations, dividing it into four items: investigation, registration, introduction, and guidance. I will describe them in order: (1) Investigation, focusing on the supply and demand of talent. On the one hand, we are constantly conducting detailed investigations into the situation of central government, local governments, public and private organizations, cultural institutions, and industrial institutions that need academic talent. On the other hand, we are also constantly conducting detailed investigations into job seekers and employees among academic talents across the country, making records, compiling statistics, and deducing the relationship between supply and demand. The office has now drafted more than 20 kinds of forms and sent them to various public and private institutions across the country for investigation. Due to the wide range, it is feared that it will not be effective in the short term. If the government and all sectors of society actively support it, the progress will be very smooth."

Registration. "(2) Registration includes graduates of schools above the specialized level and specialized researchers. Among them, job seekers should be allowed to register to facilitate introduction, and the office will also register and preserve those who are currently employed based on the information obtained from the investigation, so that they can be checked at any time. Currently, it is estimated that about 1,000 people have been registered for job seeking and employment."

Employment Introduction. "(3) Employment introduction is one of the most important tasks of this office. When society lacks correct standards for employment, it is naturally difficult to proceed. However, this office strives for caution. Unless it is a suitable candidate, it will never introduce rashly. According to the past experience of this office, the social need for talent is extremely urgent, but the difficulty of this office lies in the lack of suitable talent to supply, or the difference in treatment cannot satisfy both parties, or the employment agency simultaneously seeks people in multiple ways and cannot entrust this office exclusively. All of these are temporary phenomena. In the future, with accumulated experience, increased credibility, and a large number of registered people, we firmly believe that employment introduction can be gradually promoted. Currently, those who have been introduced to jobs account for about 40% of the total in technical fields, 35% in education, 10% in general administration, and the remaining 0.5% each in law, libraries, and academic research. The workplaces range from Ningxia in the north to Nanyang in the south. There are about 200 people who have been introduced and are still in contact. The office is also in contact with the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute and entrusts it to handle various matters related to introduction and investigation in Shanghai, which has achieved good cooperative results. In terms of the government, the Executive Yuan has issued a notice to all agencies across the country to employ the personnel introduced by this office as much as possible. In the future, administrative employment will gradually become consistent."

Internship Method. "Related to employment introduction is the internship method formulated by this office. In the past, university graduates often had a wealth of book knowledge but lacked practical experience, especially those who studied practical subjects. As a result, it was not easy to get a more satisfactory job after graduation. In the industry, university graduates are also considered incapable of being entrusted with important tasks, and are even regarded as inferior to factory apprentices. If this mentality is not fundamentally changed, the industry itself and the graduates' career paths will be greatly affected. The internship method of this office allows both parties to have the opportunity to get to know each other. The internship lasts for three months, and both parties can freely negotiate after the expiration. Currently, more than a dozen well-known factories in Shanghai have agreed to accept interns introduced by this office. The Ministry of Railways has also issued a notice to various railway bureaus to do the same. In the future, this method will be gradually implemented, which may also be a way to connect learning and application."

Guidance. "(4) Guidance is limited to job seeking, employment, and further education. This office is preparing to handle it to meet the needs. In summary, the work of this office is multifaceted, meaningful, permanent, and concrete. Its task is not only to solve the current unemployment problem of university students, but also to study the method of coordinating the entire talent, so as to eliminate the contradictory phenomenon of 'everyone looking for a job, and everything looking for someone.' However, its work is closely related to all aspects of society. Only with social cooperation, the assistance of various government agencies, the supervision of the people, and the attention of the press can it be effective."

Yu Tongkui's Speech

Next, Yu Tongkui, deputy director of the office, made a speech, briefly saying that there are two meanings for the office to host the press today: (1) To make the society understand the nature of the advisory agency. The work of introduction and guidance is important, but the investigation is even more important. We hope to achieve the goal of preparing the government to control talents. (2) In addition to hoping that the public understands this office, it is also necessary to make the public understand the pain of youth unemployment. According to the survey experience, the fault lies not in the youth themselves, but in the society creating this phenomenon. In the future, we plan to compile statistics and announce them to the society so that everyone will pay attention. However, the colleagues have limited abilities, and we hope that the press will give guidance.

Ma Chonggan's Speech. Finally, Ma Chonggan from the Shen Bao made a speech, briefly saying that the work of the Academic Work Advisory Office is the cause of all the people, and the responsibility of conveying and promoting it lies with the press. However, I have a few thoughts: (1) Talents are too concentrated. More knowledgeable people come to the cities, and only women and children are left in the countryside. (2) Schools are mostly concentrated in Shanghai, Beiping, and other places. Students from the inland come to Shanghai and Beiping to study, and most of them are unwilling to return to the inland to serve after graduation. Therefore, I hope that the Advisory Office will set up more branch offices in various provinces to investigate talents on the one hand and supply talents on the other hand, so that they can be popularized. Furthermore, those who are employed often cannot enjoy their work. Once they are tempted by material things, their morals are destroyed. The reasons for unemployment are mostly like this. Therefore, I hope that the Advisory Office should also guide them to settle down after introducing employment achievements.

Shen Bao Circulation Library Hosts a Banquet for Special Committee Members of the Reading Guidance Department 159

Newly Drafted One-Year Plan for the Future, Discussed Booklists for Self-Study in Various Subjects

The Shen Bao Circulation Library hosted a banquet at the YMCA on Baxianqiao Road the night before last (the 8th) at 7:00 PM for the specially appointed committee members of the library's Reading Guidance Department. Those who attended included Cai Yuanpei, Shen Xinqing, Du Dingyou, Wang Xiaoying, Chuan Donghua, Zhang Naiqi, Cao Zhongyuan, Sun Shiyi, Ding Shujing, Cao Liang, Wu Yaozong, Qian Bohan, Wang Chuntao, Guo Zixun, and others, totaling seventeen people. Li Gongquan, the director of the library, first gave a welcome speech and reported on the work of the Reading Guidance Department in the past year and the plan for the next year. He also put forward the library's reform opinions in various aspects and the booklists of national studies for various subjects compiled by the Reading Guidance Department, soliciting opinions from various experts. After the report, Cai Yuanpei immediately stood up happily and said that China had no libraries in the past, only private collections of books. Although libraries have gradually emerged later, there has never been a library as widespread among the people as the Shen Bao Circulation Library, and there has never been a Reading Guidance Department established to take on the responsibility of guiding people on how to read. Then, Shen Xinqing, an old veteran of the education community and currently serving at the Shanghai Hongying Library, Du Dingyou, a library expert, and Wang Xiaoying, the current principal of China Women's Middle School, gave speeches respectively. Next, Chuan Donghua and Chen Wangdao Sun Shiyi made many valuable suggestions on the selection and reading order in the literary booklist. Next, Du Dingyou briefly said about the booklist, saying that this kind of booklist is also common in foreign countries, and can be roughly divided into two types: one is for those who are initially learning a certain subject, so that readers know what the content and scope of a certain subject is, and the other is for those who are specializing in research to have a systematic booklist. After the meal, because everyone's interest was even stronger, dozens of experts changed to a circular seat, and everyone freely provided opinions. The discussion was still focused on the book list, and the director of the Reading Guidance Department explained in more detail the essentials of compiling the book list, briefly saying that this kind of book list is not the same as the national studies book list opened by Hu Shih and others in the past. They do not care about the actual needs of readers, and only open them subjectively. Now there are about five types opened, but it is only a part of the book list first opened by the Reading Guidance Department, which is also one of the types mentioned by Du Dingyou, and it is slightly more focused on the system. In the future, we also plan to compile some small booklists for various specialized issues. This kind of booklist is valuable in practicality, not in showing off. Compiling booklists is not the entire work of the guidance department. In addition, we have to do abstracts and continuations of various famous works to cooperate with the work of guiding the public to self-study, and not only meet the needs of readers in Shanghai, but also reach out to other places. Next, Zhang Naiqi proposed that the Shen Bao Circulation Library should contact small book stalls on the road and the secondary schools with incomplete libraries, and Ding Shujing said that the library must pay attention to those who are interested in reading but have no money to buy books. For example, there are 15,000 to 6,000 students in the current women's schools for the masses. After their studies, most of them cannot go on to further studies, so they need to have books to read to supply them. Next, Cao Liang said that in recent years, what I have been in contact with are some workers who have been forgotten by people. Their need for knowledge is even more urgent than that of ordinary petty citizens such as shop assistants and apprentices. I hope the library pays attention to this. Wang Chuntao briefly said that the YMCA is preparing to expand the existing library, and hopes that the Shen Bao Circulation Library will help it, and hopes that there will be a considerable connection between all the libraries in Shanghai. Therefore, the chairman asked Du Dingyou to report on the situation of the Shanghai Library. Du continued to report, finally saying that it is quite admirable that the Shen Bao Circulation Library can achieve such achievements in a short period of one year with very limited funds. Finally, the chairman reported on the treatment of the library staff and thanked the experts for their guidance. The meeting ended after ten o'clock.

National Language Education Promotion Association Organizes Middle School Student National Language Speech Contest 160

Preliminary round to be held at Wuben Girls' Middle School on the 17th of this month; Municipal Education Bureau orders all middle school students in the city to participate.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to municipal and registered private middle schools, stating: "According to a report from the National Language Education Promotion Association, the association, for the sake of promoting the national language construction movement, has resolved to carry out one type of work each month. In March, it plans to hold 'Middle School Student National Language Speech Contests' in Shanghai, Wuchang, and Shantou," and attached a copy of the "Measures for the Shanghai Middle School Student National Language Speech Contest," respectfully requesting that the affiliated public and private middle school students be ordered to participate in the competition. "Based on this, considering that the association is holding a national language speech contest for middle school students for the sake of promoting the national language construction movement, the request to order the affiliated public and private middle school students to participate in the competition should be approved. In addition to the instruction, the relevant competition measures are hereby issued. Each school should participate in this order. Attached are the Measures for the Shanghai Middle School Student National Language Speech Contest: 1. Purpose: The purpose of this association is to promote the popularization of the national language through national language speech competitions. 2. Location: This year, the competition will be held at Shanghai Wuben Girls' Middle School. 3. Level: The level of the contestants in this competition is limited to students from public and private junior and senior middle schools in Shanghai, divided into six groups: (1) Group A: First-year students who have completed junior middle school; (2) Group B: Second-year junior middle school students; (3) Group C: Third-year junior middle school students; (4) Group D: First-year senior middle school students; (5) Group E: Second-year senior middle school students; (6) Group F: Third-year senior middle school students. 4. Competition Method: Divided into two types: (1) Preliminary Round: Students in the same group will be divided into several groups for preliminary competitions; (2) Final Round: Selected students from each group will participate in the final competition. 5. Time: (1) Preliminary Round: Each person is limited to five minutes. When four minutes have elapsed, the timekeeper will ring the bell once to notify them. When five minutes have elapsed, the bell will be rung again to stop immediately; (2) Final Round: Each person is limited to ten minutes. When nine minutes have elapsed, the timekeeper will ring the bell once to notify them. When ten minutes have elapsed, the bell will be rung again to stop immediately. 6. Topic: To be determined by the contestant themselves (those selected in the preliminary round will use the same topic in the final round). 7. Participation: This year, the association will submit a request to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to order students from public and private junior and senior middle schools in Shanghai to participate in the competition. The number of participants from each school is limited to one person per group (participation in one or all six groups is allowed). 8. Registration: Participating students from each school should have their school principal submit the participant's name, school name, gender, age, native place, school name, level, address, etc., along with the speech manuscript, to the office of the National Language Education Promotion Association at Pingle Lane, Xizang Road, Shanghai, before March 15th. 9. Dates: (1) Preliminary Round: Starting at 8:00 AM on March 17th, contestants should report to the contestant registration office of this association at Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School to register and draw a number to determine the order of speeches. The competition ceremony will begin at 8:30 AM, and the preliminary round will begin at 9:00 AM; (2) Final Round: Starting at 8:00 AM on March 24th, junior middle school contestants selected from the preliminary round should report to the contestant registration office of this association at Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School to register and draw a number to determine the order of speeches. The final round will begin at 9:00 AM. Starting at 8:00 AM on March 31st, senior middle school contestants selected from the preliminary round should report to the contestant registration office of this association at Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School to register and draw a number to determine the order of speeches. The final round will begin at 9:00 AM. 10. Judging: (1) The judges will be appointed by this association, and one person will be publicly elected as the chairman of the preliminary and final rounds; (2) Judging standards and scoring methods: (A) Substance: Thought 15 points, Structure 15 points, Vocabulary 10 points, Grammar 10 points, Total 50 points; (B) Form: Voice 15 points, Intonation 15 points, Expression 10 points, Action 10 points, Total 50 points. 11. Prizes: Divided into individual prizes and association prizes: (1) Association Prizes: The five contestants with the highest scores in each group will each receive a certificate of award; (2) Individual Prizes: To be collected from all sectors of society by this association and evenly distributed to the winners of each group. 12. Supplementary Provisions: If there are any matters not covered in these measures, the National Language Education Promotion Association will revise them."

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Little Teacher 163

— Hanyu

Children! You are all students. But there is no definite boundary between students and teachers. You can be students on the one hand, but you can also be little teachers on the other!

The first condition for us to accept knowledge is literacy. If we cannot read, how can we accept a large amount of knowledge? Even if we get some information by ear, it is very limited. And everyone needs knowledge, so literacy is a necessary tool for everyone.

How few literate people there are in our country! Only two out of every ten people can read. How can such a country accept modern culture? Therefore, universal education is the most crucial task now.

Mr. Tao Xingzhi recently advocated the method of universal education is the little teacher system. That is to change primary school students into little teachers to teach illiterate people, so that illiterate people can read and accept a large amount of knowledge.

From the perspective of children, of course, they are studying; but compared with illiterate people, you are already very knowledgeable people. You are one of the three-tenths of the literate people. You should pass on the knowledge you have gained to the illiterate people, so that the illiterate people can read and have more opportunities to accept knowledge. First, you must educate the illiterate people in your family, and then expand to other families. This is fulfilling your responsibilities. Children! Arise! Strive!

How to Be a "Little Teacher" 164

— Ms. Bei Tan

Dear children, look at the name "Little Teacher", how crisp and pleasant it is! If someone calls you "Little Teacher", you must be very happy. In fact, we should know that the name "Little Teacher" is a bit difficult to bear!

Who teaches you to read? Of course, it is the "teacher"! Then aren't the "teachers" teaching you enthusiastically every day? Teaching you how to write, read, do arithmetic, sing, draw, and what games, etc., that's what "teachers" do. It's not like Zhang San who sells sweets, or Li Si who is the doorman at the school, who are worthy of being called "teachers". "Teachers" are very dignified and polite, and they are very kind.

"Little teacher", it's exactly the same as "teacher". However, when people have any doubts or things they don't understand and come to ask you "little teacher", you should answer them with the same sincere attitude that the teacher teaches you; otherwise, you are not worthy of being a "little teacher"!

Although, sometimes you may not be able to answer other people's questions, or perhaps you have never known them before, haha, don't worry, don't say teachers, even saints will sometimes be stumped by people and unable to answer.

"Little teachers" should have noble manners, upright attitudes, as well as decisive, confident, frank, honest, careful, agile, and other advantages.

Our weapons,

Brains, brains.

Water Cleanliness 166

— Zhen

Ling and Li are a pair of very close sisters. Ling is two years older than Li, and her grade is one level higher than her sister, so she understands things very well, and she helps her mother with some odd jobs at home.

One day, her mother asked her to fetch a bucket of water. A bucket of water is very heavy, so she asked her sister to help her, and then they took the bucket of water to the kitchen.

"Sister Ling, look, this bucket of water is very clean, but the teacher at school said: "There are many bacteria in it." Is it true?"

"Yes, if we had a microscope, we could take a drop of water and put it in the microscope, and we would see countless bacteria."

"Then let's pour it out! If we boil this water, won't there still be bacteria?"

"Don't pour it out, just boil it. Because when it's boiled, all these bacteria will be killed. It doesn't matter if you eat dead bacteria."

"Boiling, no way! Is there any other way?"

"There are three other methods: 1. Filtration: Use a sand filter jar, which is filled with a layer of sand and a layer of charcoal chips. The water is filtered down from the top, and it is very clean and can be drunk. 2. Distillation: Heat the water, and when the water is hot, it will turn into gas, called water vapor. When water vapor encounters cold, it turns back into water. This kind of water is the cleanest. 3. Chemical treatment: If we want to make a pond of water clean, can we use the previous two methods? It feels too troublesome. We can use chemical treatment. Just put alum and other chemical drugs in a pond of water, and after a while, the water in the pond will be very clean."

Strange Fish 167

— Bingyu

Fish are inherently aquatic, but there are surprisingly strange fish, such as "flying fish," also known as shark, which seem to be able to fly into the air like birds, and "tree-climbing fish," which seem to be able to climb trees like beasts. The "Ishuili fish" that live on the seabed have pectoral and pelvic fins that are shaped like feet and walk very fast. This fish often comes out of the water and climbs onto the sandy beach or the rocks of the island to rest, jumping around like frogs. South of Tokyo Bay, when the tide recedes, you can see these fish. Also, in the Ariake Bay of Kyushu, Japan, there is a kind of "Mochigoro" fish that can also jump freely on the sand. The sharks in the South Seas reproduce in large numbers and are particularly strange. When the weather is clear, they will fly to the branches of trees by the sea. If they see someone coming, they will immediately fly into the sea. The "walking fish" produced in India, Australia, and Africa have mouths like frogs, and their eyeballs bulge and are free. Although they are small in size, if they are kept in a pond, they will also climb onto artificial hills. Other examples include the butterfly fish of Burma and Ceylon, which often come out of the water and fly into the air.

A Blind Man Walked By 168

— Yuting

Flying Kites 169

— Wang Shouqiu

Spring is here! Spring is here! Children are busy flying kites again with great joy! As for kites, it seems we can talk about them:

Kites are made of paper and bamboo strips, so they are also called paper kites. They come in many shapes, including beauties, goldfish, centipedes, swallows... They are truly colorful and too numerous to mention. The most common one is made of two bamboo strips crossed, with a piece of paper pasted on top, and two paper strips attached below, with a string tied on, and that's a kite! This kind of kite can be bought for just two or three copper coins, but I think children can make a few of their own, wouldn't that be more economical? However, although they are the same kites, because of the skill of the person who made them, some can be raised as soon as they are released, while others cannot be raised no matter how many times they are released. This is because the four corners of the kite are different in weight, so this phenomenon occurs. If the four corners of the kite are uneven in weight, even if it can be raised, it will still tumble!

Larger kites can have a bowstring hung on them. When placed in the air, the pressure of the wind can cause the bow to make a clear sound, which is also pleasant to hear. Some people even light candles on the kites. However, these are not for children to play with. Children are too weak and can only fly small kites!

It is said that kites should be flown before Qingming, because the wind before Qingming is upward, and the wind after Qingming is downward, so you can't fly kites after Qingming!

Children's Science Lecture: The Colors of Insects 170

— Linyin

Why do insects always have colors on their bodies? Why are their colors all different? These are questions worth studying for us, and they are also interesting questions. But simply put, insects need to have colors for the following four reasons:

(1) In order to defend and attack, the colors on their bodies are often the same as the colors of the places they live in. This kind of color is called protective coloration. For example, the Lissus often lives on the grassland, so the color of its body is green. Although the color of the surface of the butterfly is beautiful, when it is still, it has the same color as the branches. The leaf butterfly produced in Ryukyu also resembles a withered leaf when it is still (Figure 1). After insects have protective coloration, it is not easy for other animals to recognize them, thus ensuring the safety of their lives.

(2) Also for the purpose of defense and attack, the colors on their bodies simulate the colors and shapes of other animals or branches. For example, bees have poisonous needles that can protect their lives, so thin-waisted flies imitate the shape and color of bees. Inchworms mimic branches (Figure 2). This is called mimicry, borrowing the colors and shapes of other animals to protect themselves.

(3) Warning other animals not to invade, special colors are displayed on the body, this color is called warning color. For example, bees have poisonous needles, and ground beetles have evil tools. These insects are not eaten by other animals, so they have a color to warn other animals. Ground beetles have long hairs, bees have colors, and ground beetles are gold-green, all of which are their characteristics (Figure 3).

(4) This function is not only found in insects, but also in other animals. That is the choice of color between males and females. They each have unique colors to attract the love of the opposite sex. For example, the male and female insects of the small purple butterfly and the small gray butterfly all have extremely beautiful colors. The colors of the male and female insects of the leopard-legged mosquito are also completely different, and often the males are more beautiful than the females (Figure 4).

Children, you think, insects are the most humble of animals, but they also have various needs like human beings, do you find it amazing?

Homemade Tank 171

— Hengjiu Qianzhuo

Explanation children! Do you know what a tank is? This was invented during the European War, and there are many styles. Its only function is to be able to carry guns and soldiers, crawl over uneven places, and destroy enemy trenches. It is the most powerful machine in war. Now someone has invented an amphibious tank, which is even more effective. Children! Here, I will teach you how to make a small tank, okay?

How to make it: First take two thread spools and file them into a serrated shape. Then nail a small nail on the side (Figure 1); then drill two holes in a small piece of wax candle (Figure 2) and connect it to the thread spool with a thicker rubber band, and fasten it on the small nails on both sides (Figure 3); then insert a large nail as shown in (Figure 4), and the machine of the tank is successfully made. Then, according to the length and thickness of the thread spool in Figure 3, make a car body (Figure 5), and add colors and names, and you are done (Figure 6).

How to play: Rotate the large nail on the machine to tighten the rubber band, cover the car body, and it will move slowly. Even if it is placed on a high and uneven place, it can crawl like a real one.

Note: (1) The rubber band cannot be too short or too long, it should be slightly shorter than the length of the thread spool and candle; (2) The rubber band cannot be twisted too tightly, because it is easy to break if it is too tight; (3) Rotate the large nail outward.

The Yellow Cat Also Agrees to Use National Products 172

— Zhiyuan

Xin'er and many classmates and children were discussing the issue of using national products at home. Xin'er said: "This year is the student national product year. Since we are students, unlike those who have not received education, we should of course use national products; now that it is designated as the student national product year, which is to promote the awakening of students, we should use national products even more; especially we primary school students, everyone likes to buy some toys to play with. If we buy toys this year, we must check carefully to see if they are national products before buying..." While speaking, a big yellow cat raised by Xin'er's family suddenly jumped onto the table and repeatedly called "Miao—Miao—". Xin'er stroked the yellow cat and said: "Cat! Do you also agree to use national products?" The yellow cat seemed to agree and called "Miao—Miao—". Many children clapped their hands and cheered, "The yellow cat also agrees to use national products and repeatedly calls 'Miao'!" Xin'er then said: "This yellow cat of mine not only agrees verbally, but is indeed a practitioner who loves to use national products. I mixed the oriental fish that I mistakenly bought in previous years with rice and gave it to it, but it would leave it and not eat it after only smelling it. It would only eat one or two bites reluctantly when it was really hungry, as if it couldn't swallow it. But if I use fresh national fish steamed and mixed with rice, it eats it with relish and doesn't look up for a long time. You see how patriotic it is! Last year, the import of foreign seafood was reported to be more than 20 million yuan. A group of unpatriotic people only care about their appetite and don't care about the leakage, which is really not as good as my yellow cat." The yellow cat heard the little master call its name and responded as if agreeing and called "Sha—Miao—".

Fairy Tale 173

— Qian Pei

(1) The elephant brothers took a big meteor and ran to the wild to set it off;

(2) On the way, they met Mr. Sheep. He widened his eyes and snatched it without asking why;

(3) Mr. Sheep stole the meteor and walked away happily. The elephant brothers were so anxious that they had no choice. The clever dog brother took the fire and hurriedly ran up to light the fuse;

(4) Things just snatched from other people's hands are held extra tightly. The fuse was lit, and the meteor shot straight out, and Mr. Sheep went with it.

Acknowledge to Mr. Huang Jingzhen and Mr. Zheng Baozhen, I am aware of your great teachings, I am grateful to you for informing me that the "Student National Product Year Song" published in our journal was broadcast by the Central Radio Station a few days ago. However, the addition of a music score may not be something that Mr. Zhang can do. I will wait for a domestic music expert to do it for him. I hereby reply and wish you well. Respectfully reply from your younger brother Dujuan.

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (9) 174

— Xinqing

The black man came back and killed another of our friends to feed himself. He slept until the next morning and then went out as he had the first time. Of course, we went out every day to get fruit and grass for food, otherwise we might have died.

We were extremely afraid, and my friends all said they wanted to end their lives voluntarily. But I had a plan and told them about it, and we decided to try it.

I said, "Friends, you know we can find a lot of wood. Now let's make a raft out of this wood and put it on the water, and we can use it temporarily. If all goes well and our black enemy dies, then we can stay on the island and wait for a ship to take us back to our hometown. If my plan fails, then we have to hurry up and take our raft out to sea. I know it's taking a great risk, but none of us want to be the next meal for this man."

Night fell again, and our enemy came back and made another friend into a meal. Then he slept, and as soon as we heard his snoring, the ten of us who were left each took a red-hot iron fork. Then we crawled up to the enemy and stabbed each of his eyes with the iron forks, blinding him.

The pain made him scream; he rose up in great anger, groping around to catch us and kill us all, but we still avoided him. Then he groped for the door and went out.

After he left, we hurried to the shore, got on the raft, and sailed out to sea. We decided to wait until dawn to see if the black man was dead, and if so, we would stay on the island.

Dawn came, and the enemy came with it, but two other people as tall as him came with him. When they saw us, they threw large rocks at our rafts. They aimed very accurately, and all the rafts were sunk except for mine, and all my friends were lost except for two.

We hurriedly sailed back out to sea and spent the night on the waves. That night, a big storm broke out, the sea was very rough, and we were hit by big waves from time to time, thinking that our raft was going to break and sink. By dawn, the storm had passed, and our raft was thrown onto a beautiful island, and we were very happy to find that the trees were full of good fruit.

Yarn and Cotton: Yarn and Cotton Market in Stagnant Condition Again 181

The yarn market is stagnant again, but the bull companies are becoming more determined as their positions gradually shrink. They are reluctant to release locked-in profits. However, the overall trend seems to be weakening, coupled with the daily decline in foreign yarn prices. Japanese companies sell yarn whenever the price rises. It is estimated that their short positions amount to 20,000 bales, and they will continue to hedge monthly. The yarn market is under immense pressure.

Few buyers for long-term yarn: Before the opening of the marked yarn market, most people expected the price to rise, as the gold market rose again and there were many rumors in the market. Therefore, the market opened slightly higher, and bull companies continued to buy. However, the market suddenly fell after the second or third sessions. Public Tendency to Sell American Cotton 183

Yesterday, when the American cotton market opened, due to 1,200 bales of delivery notices for the March contract, bullish investors turned to selling. In addition, foreign firms sold their term contracts, causing each month's price to fall by one to four points. Subsequently, inter-dealer buying provided some firmness, but long-term bullish investors gradually liquidated their positions, leading to a loosening of sentiment. New Orleans and local dealers tended to sell because of rain forecasts in West Texas and Oklahoma. Public demand was flat, and market prices were uncertain. New cotton monthly contracts were very weak due to rumors that the government might hold 5.5 million bales, preventing cotton from being pledged this season. Heisd estimates this week's cotton withdrawals at 183,000 bales, with Liverpool stocks at 316,000 bales. The closing was flat and weak, with spot prices falling by 5 points and futures falling by 2 to 8 points. The British cotton market was sluggish, with spot prices down 2 points and futures down 4 to 5 points. Indian cotton was bought by European exporters, but this was offset by large-scale selling by futures traders and liquidation by bullish investors. Prices later recovered due to cross-buying. Flat Guord Electric fell 2 rupees, and Olaum and Bai Luo Creek fell 2.25 rupees. The original electric record is on the left (dated the 8th).

The number of shipments from inland factories had also decreased, but because the exchange rate was unfavorable, most people were waiting and watching. Looking at the future, after a big drop, the rebound has already approached a corner, and it is feared that it will have to hover again. As a result, the current month was slightly down by half a point, April was slightly down by 0.25, May was slightly down by 0.75, June was slightly down by half a point, July was slightly down by 0.75, and August was slightly down by half a point.
